### Oracle Fusion Talent Management Suite

**Capability Statement | APPSolve | Oracle Business Unit**
*Document ID: W3S1-002-ORA-TalentMgmt | Version: 1.2 Approved | Wave 3*

---

#### Section 1 — APPSolve Oracle HCM Practice — Talent Management

APPSolve is an **Oracle Level 1 Partner** with a published Oracle Fusion Cloud HCM Core expertise certification on the Oracle Partner Network (OPN). With over 23 years of Oracle consulting experience, APPSolve's Oracle HCM practice includes deep capability across the Oracle Fusion Talent Management suite — encompassing Talent Profiles, Goal Management, Performance Management, Talent Review, Career Development, and Succession Planning.

**APPSolve has experience implementing Oracle Fusion Talent Management capabilities including Talent Profiles, Goal Management, Performance Management, Career Development, and Succession Planning.** This experience is underpinned by confirmed live implementations for enterprise clients, delivered using Oracle's OUM methodology and Oracle Integration Cloud (OIC) as the standard integration layer.

Oracle Fusion Talent Management is implemented in the second phase of every APPSolve Oracle HCM engagement — after Oracle HCM Core (Global HR) has been established and stabilised. The HCM Core foundation (organisational structures, worker records, job profiles) is a mandatory prerequisite: Talent Management builds directly on it. APPSolve sequences the implementation this way to ensure that talent processes operate on an accurate, complete, and correctly structured people data foundation.

**Key practice credentials for this capability:**

| Credential | Detail |
|---|---|
| Oracle partner tier | Oracle Level 1 Partner |
| Published OPN expertise | Oracle Fusion Cloud HCM Core (certified — includes Talent Management) |
| Integration expertise | Oracle Integration (OIC) — published OPN expertise area |
| Company experience | Over 23 years of Oracle consulting |
| Talent Management reference | Hollywood Bets — Talent Management, Performance Management, Goal Management, Career Development, and Succession Planning — live July 2025 |
| Prerequisite statement | See W3S1-001 Oracle HCM Core — Global HR |

---

#### Section 2 — Oracle Fusion Talent Management Suite Overview

##### 2.1 Suite Positioning

Oracle Fusion Talent Management is a suite of integrated modules within Oracle Fusion Human Capital Management, designed to enable organisations to identify, develop, measure, and retain talent systematically. APPSolve implements the Talent Management suite as a cohesive capability — not as isolated modules — ensuring that talent data, performance outcomes, succession decisions, and development plans are connected and mutually reinforcing.

The modules within the Oracle Fusion Talent Management suite that APPSolve implements include:

| Module | Core purpose |
|---|---|
| **Talent Profiles** | Defines the skills, competencies, qualifications, and experience expected for each role and recorded for each worker |
| **Goal Management** | Enables corporate-to-individual goal cascading, SMART goal setting, and ongoing progress tracking |
| **Performance Management** | Structures performance review cycles — mid-year, year-end, and ongoing feedback |
| **Talent Review** | Provides manager and HR visibility of talent population across performance and potential dimensions |
| **Career Development** | Supports employee career planning, development objectives, and internal mobility |
| **Succession Planning** | Identifies successors for key roles and tracks readiness and development of the succession pipeline |

##### 2.2 Platform Foundation

The Oracle Fusion Talent Management suite operates on the same cloud-native SaaS infrastructure as Oracle HCM Core — receiving automatic quarterly feature releases, benefiting from Oracle's ongoing AI and platform investment, and operating within the same security, privacy, and audit framework. APPSolve manages talent module configuration and quarterly release assessment alongside the client's broader Oracle HCM estate.

##### 2.3 AI-Assisted Talent Capabilities

Oracle Fusion Talent Management incorporates AI-assisted features that APPSolve activates and configures as part of the talent module implementation:

- **AI skill recommendations** — Oracle's embedded AI analyses worker profiles, learning completions, and career goals to suggest relevant skill development priorities
- **Talent search and matching** — AI-powered search surfaces workers whose profiles most closely match a target role or opportunity
- **Performance calibration support** — AI-assisted tools flag potential rating bias patterns during calibration sessions, supporting more objective talent assessments

*Note: AI feature availability and specific capability is subject to Oracle's quarterly release schedule and the client's Oracle SaaS subscription tier. APPSolve advises clients on feature activation timing as part of release management services. All AI capabilities referenced here are Oracle Fusion HCM platform capabilities; they do not represent APPSolve-developed AI functionality.*

##### 2.4 HCM Core Dependency

All Oracle Fusion Talent Management modules depend on Oracle HCM Core being implemented first. The organisational model, job profiles, position hierarchy, and worker records created in the HCM Core phase are the foundation that Talent Management reads, extends, and enriches. APPSolve does not implement Talent Management as a standalone capability — it is always sequenced after, and dependent on, a stable and validated HCM Core environment.

*See W3S1-001 Oracle HCM Core — Global HR and Employee Lifecycle for the foundational capability statement.*

---

#### Section 3 — Talent Profiles and Job Profiles

##### 3.1 The Talent Profile Foundation

Talent profiles are the architectural foundation of the Oracle Fusion Talent Management suite. Every talent process — performance reviews, goal setting, succession planning, career development — references and contributes to the talent profile. APPSolve treats talent profile design as the most consequential configuration decision in a Talent Management engagement: a well-designed profile structure enables all subsequent talent processes to function accurately; a poorly designed one creates rework that propagates across every module.

APPSolve's approach: talent profile design is completed, workshopped, and signed off before any other talent module configuration begins.

##### 3.2 Person Profiles

APPSolve configures Oracle Fusion HCM person profiles to capture the skills, competencies, qualifications, certifications, experience, and accomplishments of each worker:

| Profile element | Description |
|---|---|
| Skills and competencies | Worker-declared and manager-validated skill and competency ratings against the client's competency framework |
| Qualifications and education | Degrees, diplomas, professional qualifications, and academic achievements |
| Certifications and licences | Professional registrations, trade certificates, safety certifications — with expiry tracking |
| Work experience | Internal and external experience history; key roles and responsibilities |
| Languages | Language proficiency ratings |
| Accomplishments | Awards, recognition, publications, project achievements |
| Risk and impact | Risk-of-loss and impact-of-loss indicators populated from talent review assessments |

Worker self-service enables employees to maintain and update their own profile data, with manager and HR visibility and validation controls. Profile completeness dashboards allow HR to track adoption and identify workers with incomplete talent records.

##### 3.3 Job Profiles

APPSolve configures job profiles to define the required skills, competencies, qualifications, and experience for each role in the organisation. Job profiles serve as the benchmark against which worker profiles are compared — enabling skill gap analysis, internal talent matching, recruiting requirement definition, and succession eligibility assessment.

**Job profile components APPSolve configures:**

| Component | Purpose |
|---|---|
| Required competencies and proficiency levels | Defines the competency expectations for the role |
| Required qualifications | Educational and professional qualification requirements |
| Required certifications | Mandatory licences, registrations, or safety certifications |
| Preferred skills | Skills that are advantageous but not mandatory |
| Job family and career stream alignment | Links the job profile into the career pathway architecture |

Job profiles are configured collaboratively with the client's HR and talent leadership during the Talent Design Workshop phase of the implementation.

##### 3.4 Profile Matching and Talent Search

With both person profiles and job profiles configured, Oracle Fusion HCM provides real-time talent search and matching:

- **Internal talent search** — HR and talent leaders can search for workers whose profiles match a target job profile or a specified set of skills
- **Gap analysis** — the system identifies the delta between a worker's current profile and the requirements of a target role, informing development plan priorities
- **Succession matching** — the succession planning module uses job profile requirements to assess readiness and suitability of succession candidates

---

#### Section 4 — Goal Management

##### 4.1 Goal Frameworks

APPSolve implements Oracle Fusion Goal Management to provide a structured, organisation-wide approach to goal setting, cascading, and tracking. The goal framework is designed in collaboration with the client's HR and business leadership to ensure it reflects the organisation's performance management philosophy and review calendar.

**Goal framework elements APPSolve configures:**

| Element | Configuration |
|---|---|
| Goal plan types | Corporate, BU, team, and individual goal plans — configured per review cycle |
| Goal libraries | Pre-approved goal templates that employees and managers select from, reducing effort and ensuring alignment |
| Goal cascading | Corporate strategic objectives cascade down to BU, team, and individual level |
| SMART goal structure | Configurable goal fields — specific, measurable, time-bound, with target dates and achievement tracking |
| Goal weights | Weighted goal plans where goals carry relative importance scores that feed the performance score calculation |
| Goal approval workflows | Manager or HR approval for goal additions, changes, and closures |

##### 4.2 Progress Tracking and Check-ins

APPSolve configures Oracle Fusion Goal Management to support ongoing progress tracking throughout the review cycle, not only at formal review points:

- **Progress updates** — employees update goal progress status and percentage completion on a self-service basis
- **Manager visibility** — managers see real-time goal status for all direct reports from their manager dashboard
- **Check-in conversations** — structured check-in records can be logged against each goal, creating an ongoing coaching record
- **Automated alerts** — notifications trigger for goals approaching target dates without progress updates

##### 4.3 Goal Sharing and Cross-Team Alignment

Where the client's operating model requires cross-functional goal alignment, APPSolve configures shared goal functionality — enabling a goal owned by one team to be visible to and tracked by related teams — supporting matrix-structured organisations and project-based environments.

##### 4.4 Goal and Performance Integration

APPSolve configures the integration between Goal Management and Performance Management so that goal plan completion and achievement ratings automatically populate the performance review form. This eliminates manual re-entry and ensures that the performance rating reflects actual goal outcomes — not a separate, parallel assessment.

---

#### Section 5 — Performance Management

##### 5.1 Performance Review Cycle Configuration

APPSolve implements Oracle Fusion Performance Management to structure and automate the client's performance review process. The review cycle configuration is one of the most closely customised aspects of any HCM implementation — APPSolve dedicates a full workshop session to mapping the client's existing performance process before designing the Oracle configuration.

**Review cycle elements APPSolve configures:**

| Element | Configuration |
|---|---|
| Review cycle types | Annual, mid-year, quarterly, probation, and ad hoc cycles — each independently configured |
| Performance document | The review form template — sections, questions, rating scales, goal plan sections, narrative fields |
| Rating scales | Configurable 3-, 4-, or 5-point scales with descriptors per rating level |
| Participant roles | Employee self-assessment, manager assessment, matrix manager, HR, and skip-level sections |
| Workflow | The sequence of steps — self-assessment → manager assessment → calibration → approval → acknowledgement |
| Section weighting | Relative weighting of competency, goal, and overall rating sections |
| Timeline | Configurable start dates, step deadlines, and escalation rules |

##### 5.2 Competency Assessment

APPSolve integrates the client's competency framework into the performance review form so that the review captures both goal achievement and behavioural demonstration:

- Competencies drawn directly from the job profile for the worker's current role
- Rating of each competency against the configured scale
- Narrative evidence fields for each competency rating
- Competency ratings feed the overall performance score according to the configured weighting

##### 5.3 360-Degree Feedback

360-degree feedback is a standard Oracle Fusion Performance Management capability that APPSolve configures as part of the Talent Management engagement. APPSolve configures Oracle Fusion's participant feedback functionality to solicit structured input from peers, direct reports, and stakeholders — providing a multi-source view of each worker's performance and behaviour that enriches the manager's assessment.

**Standard 360 configuration APPSolve delivers:**

- **Participant selection** — the feedback requester (employee or manager) nominates raters; HR or the manager approves the participant list
- **Questionnaire design** — competency-based questionnaire aligned to the client's performance model; APPSolve configures the questions and rating scales in the Performance Design Workshop
- **Attribution model** — feedback may be configured as attributed (rater name visible) or anonymous (aggregated), depending on the client's governance preference
- **Aggregated results** — 360 feedback responses are presented to the manager and employee in aggregated form within the performance review form
- **Integration with review** — the 360 result feeds directly into the performance document alongside the manager assessment and self-assessment

**Configuration decisions confirmed in the Performance Design Workshop:** number of rater types; minimum and maximum participants per rater category; attribution vs anonymity; questionnaire structure; feedback window timing within the review cycle.

*Note: Advanced customer-specific workflow extensions, bespoke review processes, or non-standard 360 architectures that cannot be accommodated within Oracle standard functionality may require separate scoping.*

##### 5.4 Performance Calibration

APPSolve configures Oracle Fusion's talent calibration functionality to support the performance calibration process:

- **Calibration dashboards** — HR and talent leaders see the full population on a configurable matrix (typically performance vs potential — the 9-box)
- **Live adjustments** — managers and HR can adjust ratings during the calibration session from within the Oracle UI, with changes reflected in the worker's performance record
- **Distribution visibility** — rating distribution by department, grade, or business unit is displayed in real time, supporting normative calibration
- **Audit trail** — all calibration adjustments are recorded with the reviewer identity and timestamp

##### 5.5 Performance and Compensation Integration

Where Oracle Fusion Workforce Compensation (W3S1-005) is in scope, APPSolve configures the integration between Performance Management and Compensation so that the performance rating automatically populates the compensation planning worksheet. This enables compensation managers to allocate salary increases, bonuses, and equity awards within approved budgets — informed by performance outcome.

---

#### Section 6 — Talent Review and Succession Planning

##### 6.1 Talent Review

APPSolve implements Oracle Fusion Talent Review to give HR leaders and senior managers a structured, data-driven view of the talent population — enabling informed decisions about development, deployment, retention, and succession.

**Talent review configuration APPSolve delivers:**

| Component | Description |
|---|---|
| 9-box matrix | Performance vs potential matrix — APPSolve configures the axes, thresholds, and quadrant labels to the client's model |
| Population scope | Configurable scope — the review may cover the full organisation, a specific business unit, a grade band, or a leadership population |
| Talent indicators | Risk of loss, impact of loss, mobility preference, promotability rating — all configured and visible on the talent card |
| Talent notes | Private HR and manager notes attached to each worker's talent record, visible to authorised reviewers |
| Action plans | Post-review action items linked to the worker record — feeding development plans and succession updates |

##### 6.2 Succession Planning

APPSolve implements Oracle Fusion Succession Planning to enable the client to identify successors for key roles and manage the readiness and development of the succession pipeline.

**Succession planning capability APPSolve configures:**

| Capability | Description |
|---|---|
| Critical role identification | Roles designated as critical are flagged; succession plan depth is measured against each |
| Succession candidate pools | Nominated successors ranked by readiness level (Ready Now, Ready 1–2 Years, Ready 3+ Years) |
| Candidate profile visibility | The succession planner sees the nominee's talent card, performance history, and development plan in one view |
| Bench strength reporting | Dashboards show bench depth per critical role, by business unit, and across the organisation |
| Succession gap alerts | Roles with insufficient succession depth are highlighted for HR action |
| Incumbent comparison | Candidate profiles can be compared directly against the incumbent's and the job profile's requirements |

##### 6.3 Succession and Talent Review Integration

APPSolve configures the Talent Review and Succession Planning modules as an integrated workflow: talent review assessments (performance, potential, risk, mobility) directly inform succession candidacy decisions. A worker assessed as high-potential and ready for advancement in the talent review is surfaced automatically as a succession candidate for relevant roles, reducing administrative effort and ensuring that succession decisions are grounded in current, validated talent data.

---

#### Section 7 — Career Development

##### 7.1 Career Pathways

APPSolve implements Oracle Fusion Career Development to support employees in understanding their career options, planning their development, and taking ownership of their growth within the organisation. Career Development integrates with Talent Profiles, Goal Management, and Learning Cloud (where in scope) to create a connected talent development experience.

**Career pathway configuration APPSolve delivers:**

| Component | Description |
|---|---|
| Career pathways | Configurable career paths showing typical progressions from current role to target roles — lateral and vertical |
| Progression requirements | Skills, competencies, qualifications, and experience required at each career stage — drawn from job profiles |
| Career ladder and lattice | Linear (ladder) and cross-functional (lattice) pathways configured to reflect the client's talent strategy |
| Role exploration | Employees can explore available roles within the organisation, view requirements, and assess their readiness |

##### 7.2 Development Plans

APPSolve configures Oracle Fusion development plans to connect the skills gap identified in the talent profile to structured development actions:

- **Development goals** — linked to the employee's talent profile gaps and career pathway requirements
- **Learning activities** — formal training, on-the-job development, mentoring, and stretch assignments recorded as development actions
- **Learning Cloud integration** — where Oracle Learning Cloud is in scope, development plan actions link directly to learning programmes (see W3S1-004)
- **Manager collaboration** — development plans are co-owned by the employee and manager; both can add, edit, and review development actions
- **Progress tracking** — development goal completion is tracked against target dates and visible to HR

##### 7.3 Internal Opportunity Marketplace

APPSolve has experience implementing Oracle Opportunity Marketplace capabilities as part of broader Oracle Talent Management programmes. The Oracle Fusion Opportunity Marketplace enables employees to discover and express interest in open roles, project gigs, stretch assignments, and mentoring opportunities within the organisation — supporting internal mobility and talent retention.

**Opportunity Marketplace capabilities APPSolve implements:**

- **Role and opportunity discovery** — employees receive personalised suggestions for internal positions and assignments based on their talent profile, skills, and career interests
- **Opportunity posting** — managers and HR can post open opportunities; employees express interest and are surfaced to opportunity owners
- **Talent mobility visibility** — HR and talent leaders have real-time visibility of internal mobility interest and talent movement across the organisation
- **Recruiting integration** — the Opportunity Marketplace integrates with Oracle Recruiting Cloud (W3S1-003), distinguishing internal expressions of interest from external applications in a unified talent pipeline
- **Skills-based matching** — AI-assisted skills matching surfaces relevant opportunities based on the employee's current and aspirational skill profile

*Implementation evidence: APPSolve has experience implementing Oracle Opportunity Marketplace capabilities at enterprise clients. Do not imply universal deployment across all Oracle HCM clients.*

##### 7.4 Mentoring

Oracle Fusion Talent Management includes mentoring functionality that supports formal mentoring programmes within the career development ecosystem. Where activated, Oracle Fusion mentoring enables:

- **Mentor-mentee matching** — employees can find and request mentors based on skills, experience, and interests; or HR can facilitate matching
- **Programme tracking** — mentoring relationships, meeting logs, and development outcomes are tracked within the Oracle HCM environment
- **Relationship management** — structured mentoring journeys with goal-setting and progress visibility for both mentor and mentee

*This capability is presented as an Oracle Fusion Talent Management platform capability. APPSolve configures and activates this functionality where it is within the agreed project scope. No specific implementation reference is attached to this capability at this stage — it is cited as Oracle platform functionality that APPSolve is able to implement.*

---

#### Section 8 — APPSolve Delivery Capability — Talent Management

##### 8.1 Implementation Capability

APPSolve's Oracle HCM delivery team has certified Oracle consultants with functional expertise across the Oracle Fusion Talent Management suite. APPSolve has experience implementing Oracle Fusion Talent Management capabilities including Talent Profiles, Goal Management, Performance Management, Career Development, and Succession Planning — as evidenced by the Hollywood Bets July 2025 go-live.

**Talent Management delivery team capability:**

| Role | Capability |
|---|---|
| Principal HCM Consultant | Talent Management solution architecture; talent design workshops; calibration configuration advisory |
| Senior Functional Consultant | Module configuration across all Talent suite components; performance document design; goal framework configuration |
| Senior Technical Consultant | OIC integration (performance-to-compensation; talent-to-analytics); OTBI reporting; HCM Extracts |
| Project Manager | OUM project governance; Talent phase planning; stakeholder and HR change management |

##### 8.2 Configuration Capability

APPSolve's configuration capability across the Talent Management suite:

- **Talent profiles:** Person and job profile content sections; competency frameworks; certification tracking; profile gap analysis
- **Goal Management:** Goal plan types; goal libraries; SMART structures; cascading configuration; approval workflows; performance integration
- **Performance Management:** Performance document templates; rating scales; competency integration; workflow sequencing; calibration setup; compensation integration
- **Talent Review:** 9-box matrix; talent indicator configuration; calibration UI; action planning integration
- **Succession Planning:** Critical role designation; succession candidate pools; readiness tracking; bench strength dashboards; gap alerting
- **Career Development:** Career pathways; development plans; learning integration; internal opportunity marketplace

##### 8.3 Delivery Sequencing

APPSolve delivers the Talent Management suite in the second phase of the Oracle HCM engagement:

| Phase | Dependency | Content |
|---|---|---|
| Phase 1 — HCM Core | None | Organisational model; worker records; absence management; self-service; journeys |
| Phase 2 — Talent Management | Phase 1 complete | Talent profiles; goal framework; performance cycle; talent review; succession; career development |
| Phase 3+ — Recruiting / Learning / Compensation | Phase 1 complete; Phase 2 for some integrations | Dependent on contracted scope |

**This sequencing is non-negotiable.** Talent Management configuration references job profiles, organisational hierarchies, and worker records from HCM Core. Beginning Talent Management configuration before HCM Core is stable and validated introduces rework that disrupts both phases.

##### 8.4 Talent Design Workshops

APPSolve conducts structured Talent Design Workshops during the Journey Workshop phase, covering:

- **Talent profile design** — person profile content sections; job profile structure; competency framework alignment
- **Performance cycle design** — review cycle types; document structure; rating scale; workflow sequence; calibration approach
- **Goal framework design** — goal plan types; cascading model; SMART structure; integration with performance rating
- **Succession design** — critical role definition; candidate pool structure; readiness nomenclature; bench strength reporting requirements

Workshop outputs are documented in the Configuration Decision Log — the reference document that drives the module build.

##### 8.5 Post-Go-Live and Managed Services

APPSolve provides Talent Management managed services post-go-live:

- Ongoing performance cycle administration: opening, closing, and archiving review cycles
- Goal plan maintenance: new cycle configuration; library updates
- Talent review facilitation support: dashboard configuration for new review rounds
- Succession pool updates: readiness reassessment; new critical role additions
- Quarterly release management: Oracle feature assessment for Talent modules; activation advisory
- Reporting: OTBI talent dashboard maintenance; succession gap reports; performance distribution reports

---

#### Section 9 — Reference Implementations

##### 9.1 Hollywood Bets — Oracle Fusion Talent Management Reference

**Client:** Hollywood Bets
**Industry:** Gaming and Entertainment
**Solution:** Oracle Fusion HCM — including Talent Management, Performance Management, Goal Management, Career Development, and Succession Planning
**Go-live:** July 2025
**User count:** 7,000 users
**Status:** Live — post-go-live support active

Hollywood Bets is APPSolve's primary Oracle Fusion HCM reference implementation, encompassing the full talent suite. APPSolve has experience implementing Oracle Fusion Talent Management capabilities at Hollywood Bets, including Talent Profiles, Goal Management, Performance Management, Career Development, and Succession Planning — all live as part of the July 2025 go-live.

#### Section 10 — Integration Architecture

##### 10.1 Oracle Integration Cloud — Standard Integration Layer

Oracle Integration Cloud (OIC) is the mandatory, standard integration layer in every APPSolve Oracle Fusion HCM implementation, including engagements where Talent Management is in scope. OIC connects Oracle Fusion HCM to the client's payroll system, analytics environment, learning platform, and enterprise systems.

##### 10.2 HCM Core Integration (Mandatory)

The Talent Management suite operates within the same Oracle Fusion HCM instance as HCM Core — they are not separate systems requiring an interface. However, the Talent Management configuration depends on data structures created in HCM Core:

| HCM Core element | Talent Management dependency |
|---|---|
| Job profiles | Job profile requirements populate the benchmark against which talent profiles are assessed |
| Organisational hierarchy | Determines goal cascading paths; performance review routing; calibration scope |
| Worker records | Person records are the subject of every talent process |
| Position management | Succession planning identifies successors for positions |

##### 10.3 Performance to Compensation Integration

Where Oracle Fusion Workforce Compensation (W3S1-005) is in scope, APPSolve configures the integration between Performance Management and Compensation Planning:

- Performance ratings from closed review cycles are written to the compensation worksheet
- Compensation managers see performance ratings alongside salary, grade, and range information
- Pay decisions are informed by performance outcome and normalised across the population

This integration is configured by APPSolve as part of the Compensation engagement (W3S1-005) — not independently within the Talent Management scope.

##### 10.4 Talent to Learning Integration

Where Oracle Learning Cloud (W3S1-004) is in scope, APPSolve configures the integration between Career Development and Learning:

- Development plan actions are linked to learning programmes in Oracle Learning Cloud
- Learning completions update skill records in the talent profile
- Course completions can trigger development goal progress updates

##### 10.5 Reporting and Analytics

APPSolve configures Oracle Fusion HCM's embedded reporting for the Talent Management suite:

| Tool | Talent reporting use |
|---|---|
| OTBI | Performance distribution by BU/grade/manager; succession bench depth; goal completion rates; profile completeness |
| Delivered dashboards | Talent Overview, Performance Summary, Succession Pipeline — activated and personalised |
| HCM Analytics | Advanced talent workforce analytics where licensed |

---

#### Section 11 — Implementation Approach

##### 11.1 Talent Phase Sequencing

APPSolve delivers Talent Management in the second phase of the Oracle HCM engagement, after HCM Core is live and stable. The Talent phase follows the same OUM-structured delivery sequence as HCM Core:

| Step | Talent Management activity |
|---|---|
| **Talent Design Workshop** | Profile design; performance document design; goal framework design; succession model design |
| **Configuration Decision Log** | All Talent design decisions documented and signed off before build |
| **Talent Build (CRP 1)** | Full Talent configuration delivered; HR team walks through the configured talent process end-to-end |
| **Talent CRP 2** | Corrections from CRP 1 implemented; second walkthrough with stakeholders |
| **Integration Testing** | Performance-to-compensation link; talent-to-learning link; OTBI reports |
| **Talent UAT** | Client HR and talent team test full talent cycle: goal-setting → mid-year → year-end → calibration → succession update |
| **Talent Go-Live** | Talent modules activated in production; full performance cycle launched |
| **Hypercare** | Full APPSolve team support through the first complete performance cycle |

##### 11.2 Performance Cycle Timing

APPSolve plans the Talent Management go-live around the client's performance calendar. If the client's annual review cycle begins in Q1, the Talent go-live must be completed before the cycle opens. APPSolve confirms the performance calendar in the Talent Design Workshop and back-plans the project timeline accordingly.

**Rule:** Do not go live with Performance Management if the configured review cycle cannot complete at least one full cycle before the next configuration change is required. APPSolve confirms cycle timing with the client before any configuration is committed.

##### 11.3 Change Management for Talent Adoption

Talent Management represents a significant change to the employee and manager experience — more so than most other HCM modules. APPSolve's Talent change management approach:

- **Manager training** — dedicated manager sessions on goal setting, performance assessment, and the calibration process
- **Employee communication** — structured communication plan for goal-setting launch and performance cycle opening
- **Train-the-trainer** — HR super-users are trained to support managers and employees through the first cycle
- **Quick reference guides** — APPSolve produces one-page guides for the most common employee and manager actions in each module

##### 11.4 Testing

**CRP focus for Talent Management:**
APPSolve tests the end-to-end talent cycle in CRP — from profile creation through goal-setting, mid-year check-in, year-end assessment, calibration, succession nomination, and development plan creation. The CRP test script is designed to walk through a complete talent lifecycle, not individual module screens.

**UAT for Talent Management:**
APPSolve provides role-based UAT scripts for employee, manager, HR administrator, talent reviewer, and succession planner roles. UAT sign-off requires completion of a full talent cycle by client testers in the UAT environment.

---

#### Section 12 — Risk Register

| Risk ID | Risk | Likelihood | Impact | Mitigation |
|---|---|---|---|---|
| R-W2-001 | Talent profile architecture not agreed before build begins, causing rework across all talent modules | High | High | APPSolve mandates Talent Design Workshop and Configuration Decision Log sign-off before any Talent module configuration starts |
| R-W2-002 | Goal framework not aligned across the organisation — departments use inconsistent goal structures — undermining performance data comparability | Medium | High | Goal framework design is completed in a cross-functional workshop; HR sign-off required on the goal plan structure before configuration |
| R-W2-003 | HCM Core phase not fully complete and stable when Talent phase begins — causing rework on organisational model and job profiles during Talent build | Medium | High | APPSolve includes a formal HCM Core stability gate: Talent configuration does not begin until HCM Core CRP 2 sign-off is received |
| R-W2-004 | Client's performance calendar changes after Talent configuration has been committed — requiring rework on review cycle timelines | Low | Medium | Performance calendar confirmed in Talent Design Workshop and locked in the Configuration Decision Log; any changes after sign-off are treated as change requests |
| R-W2-005 | Talent review and calibration processes not modelled and tested in UAT — problems discovered in the first live calibration round | Medium | Medium | APPSolve includes a full calibration simulation in UAT — HR and talent leaders run a mock calibration session in the UAT environment before sign-off |

---

#### Section 13 — Assumptions Register

| Assumption ID | Assumption |
|---|---|
| A-W2-001 | Oracle HCM Core (W3S1-001 scope) is implemented, live, and stable before Talent Management configuration begins. Talent Management does not proceed in parallel with a structurally incomplete HCM Core. |
| A-W2-002 | Standard Oracle performance review forms satisfy the client's performance management requirements. Bespoke form design, custom sections, or non-standard workflows are out of scope unless separately agreed. |
| A-W2-003 | One performance review cycle type is configured initially. Additional cycle types (probation, quarterly, ad hoc) are out of scope unless separately agreed. |
| A-W2-004 | The client's goal framework structure — goal plan types, cascading model, and goal library content — is provided by the client's HR leadership in advance of configuration. APPSolve configures; the client provides the content. |
| A-W2-005 | Standard Oracle Fusion 360-degree feedback is included within the Talent Management scope. Advanced bespoke extensions, custom workflow architectures, or non-standard 360 processes that cannot be met by Oracle standard functionality are out of scope unless separately agreed. |
| A-W2-006 | Historical performance data migration from prior systems is out of scope. Oracle Fusion Talent Management is configured for forward-looking cycles only. |
| A-W2-007 | Succession pool management, talent review facilitation, and calibration sessions are conducted by the client's HR team, supported by APPSolve during hypercare. APPSolve configures the system; the client runs the talent processes. |
| A-W2-008 | Career pathway structures and job family architecture are aligned to the job profile configuration completed in HCM Core. Career Development configuration does not redesign the job architecture — it extends it. |

### Oracle Fusion Recruiting Cloud

**Capability Statement | APPSolve | Oracle Business Unit**
*Document ID: W3S1-003-ORA-RecruitingCloud | Version: 1.1 Approved | Wave 3*

---

#### Section 1: Statement of Capability

APPSolve implements Oracle Fusion Recruiting Cloud as part of Oracle Fusion HCM implementations, enabling organisations to attract, evaluate, and hire talent through a modern, AI-powered talent acquisition platform natively integrated with Oracle Fusion HCM.

APPSolve has implemented Oracle Fusion Recruiting Cloud at Hollywood Bets, a leading South African retail gaming and sports betting organisation. The Hollywood Bets Oracle Fusion HCM implementation — which went live in July 2025 for 7,000 users — included Recruiting Cloud as a primary delivery phase, encompassing external career site design, vacancy management, candidate selection processes, screening and shortlisting workflows, interview management, offer management, and structured onboarding. Oracle Integration Cloud (OIC) was deployed as the standard integration layer.

APPSolve has implementation and ongoing support experience with Oracle Taleo Recruiting solutions. While Oracle Recruiting Cloud is now the strategic Oracle recruiting platform, this experience demonstrates APPSolve's long-standing capability in Oracle recruitment solutions.

APPSolve is currently implementing Oracle Recruiting and Onboarding capabilities for a mining-sector client.

APPSolve's Oracle Recruiting Cloud delivery experience spans the retail and mining sectors. APPSolve supports clients across Retail, Mining, and Professional Services industries.

---

#### Section 2: Oracle Fusion Recruiting Cloud — Module Overview

Oracle Fusion Recruiting Cloud is Oracle's next-generation talent acquisition platform, forming part of the Oracle Fusion HCM suite. APPSolve configures and implements Recruiting Cloud to enable organisations to manage the full talent acquisition lifecycle — from employer branding and candidate attraction through to structured onboarding and integration with Oracle Fusion Core HR.

The platform delivers five primary value outcomes that APPSolve configures as part of every Oracle Recruiting Cloud implementation:

| Value Outcome | Description |
|---|---|
| **AI-Driven Talent Acquisition** | Oracle Recruiting Cloud applies AI and machine learning to match candidates with roles based on skills, experience, and potential. Provides intelligent recommendations to recruiters and hiring managers. |
| **Enhanced Candidate Experience** | Mobile-friendly career sites with personalised job recommendations, chatbot and virtual assistant engagement, and self-service application tracking. Configured by APPSolve to reflect the client's employer brand. |
| **Automated and Efficient Recruiting** | Automates job posting, interview scheduling, offer management, and candidate communications. Reduces administrative burden and accelerates time-to-hire. |
| **Data-Driven Recruiting Decisions** | Real-time analytics on recruiting performance, candidate pipeline status, and hiring metrics. Identifies bottlenecks and supports evidence-based hiring strategy. |
| **Seamless Integration with Oracle HCM** | Native integration with Oracle Fusion Core HR, Oracle Payroll Interface, and Oracle Onboarding. Candidate records convert to employee records in Core HR upon hire. Third-party job boards, background check providers, and assessment platforms connect via OIC and REST APIs. |

---

#### Section 3: Talent Acquisition Foundation and Platform Architecture

##### 3.1 Oracle Fusion Recruiting Cloud — Core Architecture

APPSolve implements Oracle Fusion Recruiting Cloud as an integrated talent acquisition platform within the Oracle Fusion HCM landscape. The platform serves as the applicant tracking system (ATS) of record, connecting employer branding, candidate sourcing, selection, offer management, and structured onboarding in a single Oracle-native system.

APPSolve configures the following foundation elements as part of every Recruiting Cloud implementation:

| Foundation Element | APPSolve Configuration Scope |
|---|---|
| **Hiring and selection processes** | Configurable hiring workflow stages from application through to offer; aligned to client HR operating model |
| **Job and position integration** | Job profiles, position management, and competency frameworks from Oracle Core HR drive Recruiting Cloud job postings and screening criteria |
| **User roles and access** | Recruiter, hiring manager, and HR administrator roles configured with appropriate access to candidate data, requisitions, and offer workflows |
| **Reporting and dashboards** | Oracle Recruiting Administration reports and standard Oracle HCM dashboards configured to support recruiting KPIs |
| **OIC integration architecture** | Oracle Integration Cloud deployed as the standard integration layer connecting Recruiting Cloud with third-party job boards, background check providers, and assessment platforms |

##### 3.2 Taleo Recruiting — Legacy Platform Experience

APPSolve has implementation and ongoing support experience with Oracle Taleo Recruiting solutions. While Oracle Recruiting Cloud is now the strategic Oracle recruiting platform, this experience demonstrates APPSolve's long-standing capability in Oracle recruitment solutions. Clients currently operating Oracle Taleo Recruiting environments may consult APPSolve on legacy support continuity and platform modernisation pathways.

##### 3.3 Internal Mobility

Oracle Fusion Recruiting Cloud includes an Internal Career Site capability that enables employees to search and apply for open positions within the organisation. The platform recommends internal job opportunities to employees based on skills, experience, and career interests, and tracks internal applications through configurable approval workflows.

APPSolve supports internal mobility configuration as an Oracle platform capability. Internal mobility is positioned as a complement to Oracle Talent Management and Oracle Succession Planning. Implementation evidence for Oracle Opportunity Marketplace — a dedicated internal talent marketplace — is available from APPSolve's Oracle Talent Management practice.

---

#### Section 4: Requisition and Vacancy Management

APPSolve configures Oracle Fusion Recruiting Cloud's requisition and vacancy management capabilities to align with each client's HR operating model, approval structure, and position management framework.

##### 4.1 Job Requisition Configuration

| Capability | APPSolve Configuration Approach |
|---|---|
| **Requisition creation and approval** | Managers or HR create job requisitions using predefined templates covering job descriptions, required qualifications, and salary bands. Configurable approval routing aligned to client organisational hierarchy. |
| **AI-powered job descriptions** | Oracle generative AI assists in creating engaging, compliant job descriptions from structured position data. APPSolve configures the AI job description capability and trains HR teams on its governance. |
| **Position-driven requisitions** | Requisitions are linked to Oracle Fusion Core HR position management. Open positions trigger requisition workflows automatically where configured. |
| **Template library** | APPSolve establishes a requisition template library during implementation. New requisitions are created post go-live; no historical requisition migration is performed. |

##### 4.2 Vacancy Management and Hiring Workflows

APPSolve configures end-to-end hiring workflows defining the stages through which candidates progress from application to hire. Standard APPSolve implementation includes:

- **One candidate selection process** — the framework defining stages and evaluation criteria for all roles within the implementation scope
- **One job application flow** — the candidate-facing application sequence, optimised for mobile and quick-apply interaction
- **Configurable stage transitions** — automated notifications, task assignments, and approval triggers at each hiring workflow stage
- **Recruiter and hiring manager collaboration** — shared dashboards providing real-time visibility of candidate pipeline status

---

#### Section 5: Candidate Experience and Employer Branding

APPSolve implements Oracle Fusion Recruiting Cloud's candidate experience capabilities as confirmed implemented deliverables, including branded career sites, candidate talent communities, and employee referral programmes.

##### 5.1 Branded Career Sites and Candidate Portals

APPSolve configures both external and internal career sites as part of every Oracle Recruiting Cloud implementation:

| Site Type | Configuration Scope |
|---|---|
| **External career site** | One branded external career portal per implementation scope. Configured with client logo branding in Oracle-required format. Mobile-responsive design. Branded to align with client corporate standards. Graphical web design is a client responsibility; APPSolve configures the Oracle career site framework. |
| **Internal career site** | One internal career portal for employee-facing job opportunities. Enables self-service job browsing, application submission, and application tracking by current employees. |
| **Candidate self-service** | Candidates access a personalised application tracking portal, receive automated status notifications, and can schedule interviews through self-service tools. |

The Hollywood Bets implementation included the design and configuration of external recruiting pages aligned to the Hollywood Bets corporate brand, delivered in collaboration with the client's web and marketing teams.

##### 5.2 Multi-Channel Job Posting and Candidate Sourcing

APPSolve configures Oracle Recruiting Cloud's multi-channel posting and candidate sourcing capabilities to maximise the reach of each client's talent acquisition effort:

- **Multi-channel job distribution** — automated posting to external job boards (including Indeed integration), social media, professional networks (LinkedIn), and employee self-service portals
- **LinkedIn integration** — APPSolve configures LinkedIn profile import for candidate applications and job sharing. Client LinkedIn recruiter accounts are required as a prerequisite.
- **AI candidate matching** — Oracle AI recommends best-fit candidates for open requisitions, reducing manual screening overhead and accelerating shortlisting
- **CRM-style talent pools** — APPSolve configures candidate talent communities, enabling targeted recruiting campaigns and relationship nurturing with passive candidates

##### 5.3 Employee Referral Programme

Oracle Fusion Recruiting Cloud natively integrates employee referral programme management. APPSolve configures the referral capability as part of Recruiting Cloud implementations:

- Employees refer candidates directly through the employee self-service portal
- Referred candidates populate the ATS within Oracle Recruiting Cloud alongside all other applicants
- The system tracks referred candidates through the hiring pipeline, attributing hires to referrers
- Automated notifications are sent to referrers at key hiring milestones
- Referral bonus eligibility tracking is supported through configurable rules

---

#### Section 6: Screening, Shortlisting and Interview Management

##### 6.1 Screening and Shortlisting

APPSolve configures Oracle Recruiting Cloud's automated screening and shortlisting capabilities to reduce manual effort and improve hiring quality:

| Capability | Description |
|---|---|
| **Automated resume parsing** | Oracle Recruiting Cloud parses candidate applications against job requisition criteria, extracting qualifications, skills, and experience for comparison against role requirements |
| **AI-powered candidate ranking** | AI evaluates candidate profiles against job descriptions and recommends best-fit candidates, reducing unconscious bias and accelerating screening time |
| **Knock-out criteria** | APPSolve configures mandatory and preferred criteria within hiring workflows, enabling automated screening at the application stage |
| **Pipeline stage management** | Candidate status is tracked through configurable stages (Applied → Screened → Interviewed → Offer → Hired) with full audit trail |

##### 6.2 Interview Management

APPSolve configures Oracle Recruiting Cloud's collaborative interview management tools to support structured, auditable hiring decisions:

- **Interview self-scheduling** — candidates access a self-service portal to select interview times from interviewer availability slots, reducing scheduling coordination overhead
- **Interview scorecards** — structured evaluation forms configured per role type, ensuring consistent assessment criteria across interviewers
- **Interviewer collaboration** — centralised dashboard for recruiters and hiring managers to share real-time feedback, interview notes, and hiring recommendations
- **Interview logistics** — automated invitation, confirmation, and reminder communications to candidates and interviewers at each interview stage

---

#### Section 7: Offer Management

APPSolve configures Oracle Fusion Recruiting Cloud's offer management capabilities to support structured, auditable offer processes from generation through to candidate acceptance.

##### 7.1 Offer Letter Generation and Approval

| Capability | APPSolve Configuration Approach |
|---|---|
| **Dynamic offer letters** | APPSolve configures up to three branded offer letter templates per implementation scope, reflecting role type, employment category, and client branding requirements |
| **Offer approval workflow** | Configurable approval routing for offer letters, aligned to client HR and finance authorisation structures |
| **Digital signing** | Oracle Recruiting Cloud supports digital offer acceptance; candidates receive and accept offer letters electronically through the candidate self-service portal |
| **Offer negotiation tracking** | Offer status, counter-offer interactions, and acceptance or decline outcomes are tracked within the candidate record |
| **Skill transfer** | APPSolve trains client HR teams to create and maintain offer letter templates post go-live, ensuring independence from APPSolve for ongoing offer letter management |

##### 7.2 Transition from Offer to Onboarding

Upon offer acceptance, Oracle Fusion Recruiting Cloud initiates the onboarding workflow automatically. Candidate data is converted to an employee record in Oracle Fusion Core HR, eliminating manual re-keying of information between systems. APPSolve configures the offer-to-onboarding transition as part of the Recruiting Cloud delivery scope.

---

#### Section 8: Onboarding and Preboarding

APPSolve implements Oracle Fusion Recruiting Cloud's onboarding capability as a structured, automated process spanning from offer acceptance through Day 1 integration into Oracle Fusion Core HR. Full Journeys-based lifecycle event management is addressed in W3S1-001 Oracle HCM Core.

##### 8.1 Preboarding — From Offer Acceptance to Start Date

APPSolve configures preboarding workflows enabling new hires to complete required actions before their first day:

| Preboarding Task | Configuration |
|---|---|
| **Welcome communications** | Automated welcome emails and introductory content sent upon offer acceptance |
| **Document submission** | New hires complete required documentation (employment contracts, tax forms, policy acknowledgements) through a secure self-service portal before start date |
| **System access preparation** | Onboarding task workflows trigger IT and facilities provisioning actions in parallel with HR onboarding steps |
| **Pre-arrival orientation** | New hire portal provides access to company culture content, team introductions, and pre-reading materials before Day 1 |

##### 8.2 Structured Onboarding Workflows

APPSolve configures two standard onboarding processes per implementation scope: one for pre-hires (pre-start-date activities) and one for new hires (Day 1 through induction period activities).

| Onboarding Capability | APPSolve Configuration Approach |
|---|---|
| **Automated workflow initiation** | Onboarding workflows trigger automatically upon offer acceptance in Oracle Recruiting Cloud, requiring no manual HR intervention |
| **Personalised onboarding portals** | New hires access a dedicated portal configured with role-relevant content, tasks, and progress tracking |
| **Task management** | Onboarding tasks assigned to new hires, managers, and HR with automated reminders and completion tracking |
| **Document management** | Secure collection and storage of new hire documents integrated with Oracle Fusion Core HR records |
| **Integration with Core HR** | Candidate data is seamlessly converted to employee records in Oracle Fusion Core HR upon hire, ensuring data integrity and eliminating duplicate data entry |

##### 8.3 Onboarding Reporting

Standard Oracle Recruiting Administration dashboards, configured by APPSolve during implementation, provide visibility of onboarding task completion rates, outstanding items, and new hire progress. Skills transfer to client HR teams ensures ongoing onboarding reporting independence post go-live.

---

#### Section 9: APPSolve Delivery Capability

##### 9.1 Oracle Recruiting Cloud Practice

APPSolve's Oracle Business Unit includes a dedicated team of HCM-certified consultants with implementation experience in Oracle Fusion Recruiting Cloud. APPSolve holds Oracle Level 1 Partner status.

APPSolve has implemented Oracle Fusion Recruiting Cloud at Hollywood Bets — a retail gaming and sports betting organisation with 7,000 employees — and is currently active in the mining sector delivering Oracle Recruiting and Onboarding. APPSolve also holds implementation and ongoing support experience with Oracle Taleo Recruiting solutions.

##### 9.2 Recruiting Cloud Delivery Methodology

APPSolve delivers Oracle Fusion Recruiting Cloud implementations using the Oracle Unified Methodology (OUM), adapted for Recruiting Cloud's specific design and configuration requirements.

Recruiting is typically structured as a dedicated implementation phase, following Core HCM and Talent Management. This sequencing is deliberate: the job and position framework, competency libraries, and talent profile structures established in earlier phases provide the foundation on which Recruiting Cloud configuration is built.

APPSolve's standard Recruiting Cloud delivery approach includes:

| Delivery Element | Description |
|---|---|
| **External career site design** | Designed in collaboration with the client's marketing and web teams to align with corporate brand standards. APPSolve configures the Oracle career site framework; graphical design is a client-led deliverable. |
| **Process automation** | Recruitment process automation is a core delivery objective. APPSolve conducts process design workshops to identify automation opportunities within the client's existing recruitment workflow before configuring the Oracle system. |
| **Vacancy and filtering design** | APPSolve designs HCM staff-facing tools to minimise time spent filtering applicants and compiling interview feedback, ensuring internal efficiency is delivered alongside candidate-facing experience. |
| **Training and skills transfer** | Modular training material prepared per the OUM Methodology. APPSolve trains client HR and recruiting teams to own and maintain configuration, reports, and offer letters post go-live. |

##### 9.3 Resource and Delivery Model

| Resource type | Role |
|---|---|
| HCM Principal Consultant | Design authority; configuration governance; client engagement leadership |
| HCM Senior Functional Consultant | Project implementation lead; Recruiting Cloud configuration and testing |
| HCM Senior Functional / Technical Consultant | OIC integration architecture; REST API configuration; technical build |
| Project Manager | Delivery governance; timeline management; risk and issue escalation |

Implementation is conducted remotely with on-site presence for key workshops and design sessions where required. APPSolve's hybrid delivery model is applied as standard.

#### Section 11: Integration Architecture

Oracle Integration Cloud (OIC) is APPSolve's standard integration layer in every Oracle Fusion HCM implementation, including Oracle Recruiting Cloud. This applies without exception.

##### 11.1 Standard Recruiting Cloud Integration Points

| Integration | Method | Description |
|---|---|---|
| **Oracle Fusion Core HR** | Native Oracle integration | Candidate records convert automatically to employee records in Core HR upon hire. No manual data re-entry. |
| **Oracle Fusion Payroll Interface** | OIC / HCM Extracts | New hire data flows from Recruiting Cloud through Core HR to the payroll integration layer. Third-party payroll systems (PaySpace, SAP Payroll) connected via OIC as standard. |
| **Oracle Onboarding / Journeys** | Native Oracle integration | Offer acceptance in Recruiting Cloud triggers onboarding workflows automatically. |
| **LinkedIn** | Native Oracle integration | LinkedIn profile import for candidate applications; job sharing to LinkedIn professional network. Client LinkedIn recruiter accounts required. |
| **External job boards** | OIC / REST APIs | Automated multi-channel job posting to external job boards (Indeed and equivalent). Source effectiveness tracking included. |
| **Background check providers** | REST APIs | Third-party background verification services connect via Oracle REST APIs. Provider and integration scope are client-specific. |
| **Assessment platforms** | REST APIs | Third-party candidate assessment platforms connect via REST APIs where in scope. |

##### 11.2 REST API Availability

Oracle Fusion HCM provides comprehensive RESTful APIs covering all major HCM business objects, including recruiting data (candidates, requisitions, applications, offers, onboarding tasks). APPSolve's technical team configures REST API-based integrations where standard OIC adapters are not available or where client architecture requires custom integration patterns.

---

#### Section 12: Implementation Approach

##### 12.1 Recruiting Cloud within the Oracle HCM Programme

APPSolve implements Oracle Fusion Recruiting Cloud as a structured delivery phase within the broader Oracle Fusion HCM programme. The sequencing follows the dependency model established across APPSolve implementations:

| Phase | Content | Dependency |
|---|---|---|
| Phase 1 | Core HCM — Global HR, Absence Management, Self-Service | Foundation — all subsequent phases depend on Phase 1 |
| Phase 2 | Talent Management — Talent Profiles, Goal Management, Performance, Career Development, Succession | Requires Phase 1 (employee and job structure) |
| **Phase 3** | **Oracle Recruiting Cloud** | **Requires Phase 1 (position management, job profiles, competency framework)** |
| Phase 4 | Learning Cloud, Workforce Compensation, Help Desk | Requires Phases 1–3 |

##### 12.2 OUM Delivery Phases — Recruiting Cloud

APPSolve applies the Oracle Unified Methodology (OUM) across all Oracle Fusion HCM implementations, including Recruiting Cloud:

| OUM Phase | Recruiting Cloud Activities |
|---|---|
| **Mobilize** | Project charter; scope confirmation; Recruiting Cloud configuration workbooks; resource allocation; kick-off |
| **Scope and Design** | Recruiting process workshops; hiring workflow design; career site design brief; job profile and competency framework review; integration architecture design |
| **Prototype** | CRP1 — initial configuration walk-through; stakeholder feedback; CRP2 — refined configuration including career site, offer templates, and onboarding workflows |
| **Build** | Full configuration build; OIC integration build (job boards, background check, payroll); custom reports (up to 10 reports and 6 workflows per agreed scope); training material development |
| **Deploy** | Production build; data verification; UAT; end-user training; go-live support |
| **Post Go-Live** | Hyper-care (full team approximately 3 months); steady-state handover; ongoing support optional |

##### 12.3 Standard Implementation Assumptions

The following assumptions reflect APPSolve's standard Recruiting Cloud delivery scope, drawn from confirmed implementation experience:

| Assumption ID | Assumption |
|---|---|
| A-W3-001 | Recruiting is configured as a global function — one recruitment portal serves all in-scope territories |
| A-W3-002 | One job application flow is configured per implementation scope |
| A-W3-003 | One candidate selection process (hiring workflow framework) is configured per implementation scope |
| A-W3-004 | One external career site is configured with client logo branding in Oracle-required format; graphical web design is a client responsibility |
| A-W3-005 | One internal career site is configured for employee-facing job browsing and application |
| A-W3-006 | LinkedIn integration is configured for job sharing and candidate profile import; client LinkedIn recruiter accounts are a client-provided prerequisite |
| A-W3-007 | Up to 3 offer letter templates are configured, branded as per client requirements; no requisitions are migrated — new requisitions are created by end users post go-live |
| A-W3-008 | Two onboarding processes are configured: one for pre-hires (pre-start-date activities) and one for new hires (Day 1 through induction); additional onboarding process types are out of scope unless separately agreed |
| A-W3-009 | Standard Oracle Recruiting Administration reports and dashboards satisfy reporting requirements within implementation scope; additional custom reports require separate scoping |
| A-W3-010 | Job profiles (competencies, skills, qualifications) are defined and available in Oracle Core HR prior to Recruiting Cloud configuration — Recruiting Cloud draws from the Core HR position and job framework |

---

#### Section 13: Risk Register

| Risk ID | Risk | Likelihood | Impact | Mitigation |
|---|---|---|---|---|
| R-W3-003-001 | Career site design complexity exceeds standard scope — client's brand standards require bespoke graphical design beyond Oracle career site configuration capabilities | Medium | Medium | Clarify career site design scope at project initiation. Graphical web design is a client responsibility. APPSolve configures the Oracle framework; advanced design work is scoped separately. |
| R-W3-003-002 | LinkedIn recruiter accounts not available at project start — absence of client LinkedIn accounts delays social integration configuration and testing | Low | Low | Pre-tender check: confirm client LinkedIn recruiter account availability. Flag as prerequisite in project charter at kick-off. |
| R-W3-003-003 | Job profiles and competency frameworks not ready in Core HR at the time Recruiting Cloud configuration begins — Recruiting Cloud depends on the Core HR position and job structure | Medium | High | Recruiting Cloud is sequenced as Phase 3, following Core HCM (Phase 1). Dependency must be explicitly managed in programme plan. Job profile readiness checkpoint included in Phase 2 / Phase 3 gate review. |
| R-W3-003-004 | Onboarding task ownership ambiguity — responsibilities for completing onboarding tasks (new hire, manager, HR, IT) are not defined before configuration begins, resulting in workflow re-design during UAT | Medium | Medium | Onboarding process design workshop conducted in Scope and Design phase. RACI for all onboarding task types agreed before configuration begins. |
| R-W3-003-005 | Third-party integration scope (background checks, assessments) is underestimated at tender stage — each provider has different API requirements and data exchange formats | Medium | Medium | Background check and assessment platform integrations scoped as time-and-material items. Standard REST API patterns applied where provider APIs are compliant. Provider API documentation required before integration design begins. |

---

#### Section 14: Assumptions Register

| Assumption ID | Assumption | Risk if incorrect |
|---|---|---|
| A-W3-001 | Recruiting is a global function — one portal per implementation scope | If territories require separate portals, scope increases materially; each additional portal requires separate configuration and testing |
| A-W3-002 | One job application flow per implementation scope | Additional application flows increase configuration and UAT effort; scope change required |
| A-W3-003 | One candidate selection process per implementation scope | Role-specific selection processes are a scope increase; additional processes require separate design and configuration |
| A-W3-004 | Career site branding limited to logo and basic brand elements; client provides logo in Oracle-required format | Graphical design requirements beyond Oracle framework require client web team engagement; APPSolve is not responsible for graphical web design |
| A-W3-005 | LinkedIn integration requires existing client LinkedIn recruiter accounts | Absence of accounts delays integration by the time required to establish accounts; client action required |
| A-W3-006 | Up to 3 offer letter templates; no requisition migration | Additional offer letter templates require separate scoping; historical requisition migration is not a standard Recruiting Cloud deliverable |
| A-W3-007 | Two onboarding processes in scope: pre-hire and new hire | Additional onboarding process types (e.g., contractor onboarding, re-hire onboarding) require separate scoping |
| A-W3-008 | Standard Oracle Recruiting dashboards and reports satisfy reporting requirements | Custom reports beyond standard Oracle OOB dashboards require separate scoping; up to 10 custom reports and 6 custom workflows are the standard implementation cap |
| A-W3-009 | Job profiles, competencies, skills, and qualifications are defined and ready in Oracle Core HR before Recruiting Cloud configuration begins | Delay in job profile readiness delays Phase 3 configuration start date; programme timeline risk |
| A-W3-010 | Background check and assessment platform providers are identified and their API documentation is available at the start of the integration design phase | Undisclosed provider requirements or proprietary APIs may extend integration design and build timelines |
