### Oracle Workforce Management

**Capability Statement | APPSolve | Oracle Business Unit**
*Document ID: W3S1-007-ORA-WorkforceManagement | Version: 1.1 Approved | Wave 3*

---

#### Section 1: Statement of Capability

APPSolve configures and implements Oracle Workforce Management capabilities across the full spectrum of workforce administration — from daily absence tracking and leave management through to time and labor capture, workforce scheduling, and manager self-service workforce operations.

Oracle Fusion HCM's Workforce Management suite comprises four primary capability areas that work together to provide organisations with comprehensive, rules-driven workforce administration:

| Capability Area | Module | Licensing | APPSolve positioning |
|---|---|---|---|
| **Absence Management** | Oracle Absence Management | Included in Oracle HCM | **Confirmed delivery** — standard in every Oracle HCM implementation |
| **Time and Labor** | Oracle Time and Labor | Included in Oracle HCM | **Confirmed capability (PoC evidence)** — implemented as part of a proof-of-concept programme; APPSolve has confirmed functional and technical readiness for production delivery |
| **Workforce Scheduling** | Oracle Workforce Scheduling | Included in Oracle HCM | **Platform Capability** — APPSolve can configure and implement where required and in scope |
| **Workforce Health and Safety** | Oracle Workforce Health and Safety | Included in Oracle HCM | **Platform Capability** — APPSolve can support and configure where required and in scope |

Absence Management is APPSolve's most consistently implemented Oracle Workforce Management module — it is configured as a standard Phase 1 deliverable in every Oracle Fusion HCM implementation engagement. Oracle Time and Labor has been implemented by APPSolve as part of a proof-of-concept programme for a South African retail client, confirming APPSolve's functional and technical capability to deliver T&L in production environments.

APPSolve's Oracle practice includes certified HCM consultants with implementation experience across Absence Management in retail, mining, and professional services sectors. The practice's mobile-first deployment approach enables employee self-service absence and time management from any device, reducing administrative burden on HR teams while improving data accuracy and compliance.

---

#### Section 2: Oracle Workforce Management Architecture — Module Scope and Boundaries

##### 2.1 Module Architecture

Oracle Fusion HCM Workforce Management is the collective term for the capabilities that govern how employees' time, attendance, leave, and workplace safety are managed within the Oracle HCM platform. Each capability is a configurable module within Oracle Fusion HCM.

**Module dependency and sequencing:**

Workforce Management modules are deployed following Core HR (W3S1-001). Core HR establishes the foundational structures — legal entities, business units, departments, jobs, positions, and employee records — on which all Workforce Management modules depend.

```
Core HR (W3S1-001)
    ├── Absence Management  ← Phase 1 in every HCM implementation
    ├── Time and Labor      ← Phase 2+ where in scope
    ├── Workforce Scheduling ← Where in scope
    └── Workforce H&S       ← Where in scope
```

##### 2.2 Absence Management within Workforce Management

Absence Management is the foundational Workforce Management module. It is always implemented in Phase 1 of an Oracle HCM programme, alongside Core HR. Absence Management establishes the leave framework — absence types, accrual rules, entitlements, and self-service processes — that all subsequent phases depend on.

In implementations where Time and Labor is in scope, Absence Management and Time and Labor work in conjunction: absence is tracked within Absence Management and flows to Time and Labor for accurate time validation and payroll processing.

##### 2.3 Integration Architecture

All Oracle Workforce Management modules are integrated by design within Oracle Fusion HCM. The integration architecture follows the standard APPSolve Oracle HCM deployment model:

```
Oracle Absence Management ──► Oracle Time and Labor ──► Oracle Payroll / HCM Extracts ──► OIC ──► Payroll Platform
Oracle Workforce Scheduling ──► Oracle Time and Labor (schedule drives time expectations)
Oracle HCM Mobile App ──► All modules (self-service and approval workflows)
Biometric / Access Control System ──► OIC ──► Oracle Time and Labor (time capture)
```

---

#### Section 3: Absence Management

##### 3.1 Overview

Oracle Absence Management is a comprehensive, cloud-based leave and absence management solution included within Oracle Fusion HCM. It provides organisations with a configurable, rules-driven framework to define, administer, and track all types of employee absence — from annual leave and sick leave to statutory leave types prescribed under South African labour law.

APPSolve configures and implements Oracle Absence Management as a standard deliverable in every Oracle Fusion HCM implementation. It is positioned in Phase 1 of the APPSolve implementation approach, alongside Core HR, because the leave framework underpins the entire Oracle HCM employee experience from day one of go-live.

> **Confirmed implementation reference:** APPSolve's Oracle HCM implementation for a major South African retail and gaming client (go-live July 2025, 7,000 users) included Oracle Absence Management as a Phase 1 deliverable. APPSolve is currently implementing Oracle HCM Absence Management for a mining-sector client as part of an active Oracle HCM programme.

##### 3.2 Absence Management Capabilities

| Capability | Description | Notes |
|---|---|---|
| **Absence plan configuration** | Define absence plans for each leave type — annual leave, sick leave, family responsibility, maternity, parental, study leave, bereavement, and other statutory and discretionary leave types | SA-specific plans configured per BCEA requirements |
| **Accrual rules** | Configure accrual rates, accrual frequency (daily, monthly, anniversary), and accrual caps per plan. Accruals calculated automatically based on employee tenure, grade, and assignment | APPSolve configures accrual rules as a standard design deliverable |
| **Leave entitlements** | Define minimum entitlements, carry-over rules, maximum balance caps, and expiry rules per absence type | BCEA statutory minimums enforced |
| **Multiple absence plans per employee** | Employees can hold concurrent absence plans — annual leave, sick leave, maternity simultaneously managed | Standard Oracle Fusion capability |
| **Employee self-service leave requests** | Employees submit leave requests through the Oracle HCM self-service portal or mobile app. Team calendars and personal absence balances visible at point of submission | Reduces HR administrative overhead |
| **Manager approval workflows** | Configurable approval chains — line manager, HR Business Partner, or multi-level. Managers approve, deny, or request modification from self-service or mobile app | Standard workflow — configurable per leave type |
| **Real-time balance visibility** | Employee and manager see real-time leave balances at any point. Oracle HCM calculates entitlements, consumed leave, and projected balance including pending requests | |
| **Team absence calendar** | Managers view team leave calendar to assess coverage before approving leave requests. Absence conflicts flagged | Manager self-service standard feature |
| **HR override and correction** | HR administrators can adjust leave balances, create retroactive absence records, and correct historical entries | Role-based access control governs who can adjust |
| **Absence integration with payroll** | Approved absence transactions flow to payroll (Oracle Payroll Cloud or third-party payroll via HCM Extracts or OIC) for accurate payroll processing — deductions, leave pay-outs, and absence-based payments | Standard integration in every implementation |
| **Audit trail** | Full audit trail of all absence requests, approvals, balance adjustments, and corrections | Governance and compliance standard |
| **Reporting (OTBI)** | OTBI subject areas for absence: leave balances, absence trends, leave liability, top absence types, absenteeism rate, team availability | Standard OTBI — cross-reference W3S1-006 for OAX analytics |

##### 3.3 South African Legislative Absence Requirements

APPSolve configures Oracle Absence Management to comply with South African labour legislation. Key SA statutory requirements configured as standard:

| Statutory requirement | Legislation | Configuration |
|---|---|---|
| **Annual leave** | BCEA Section 20 — minimum 15 working days per annual leave cycle (or 1.25 days per month) | Accrual plan configured per BCEA minimum; employer policies apply additional entitlements |
| **Sick leave** | BCEA Section 22 — 30 days in 3-year cycle; 1 day per 26 days worked in first 6 months | Two-tier sick leave plan configured: initial period + full cycle |
| **Family responsibility leave** | BCEA Section 27 — 3 days per year on birth, illness, or death of family members | Entitlement plan configured |
| **Maternity leave** | BCEA Section 25 — 4 consecutive months | Maternity absence plan configured; payroll treatment confirmed during design |
| **Parental leave** | BCEA Section 25A — 10 consecutive days | Parental leave plan configured |
| **Unpaid leave** | By agreement with employer | Configurable plan with nil accrual |
| **Public holidays** | Public Holidays Act — 13 SA public holidays | Oracle Fusion Work Schedules and Absence Management handle public holiday interactions |

**Legislative assumption (standing):** Legislative-specific absence requirements must be documented in a standardised format by the client before the absence plan configuration workshop. APPSolve configures plans to the agreed documented standard.

##### 3.4 Employee and Manager Self-Service

| Self-Service Capability | User | Description |
|---|---|---|
| Submit leave request | Employee | Submit any absence type through self-service portal or mobile app; view current balance before submitting |
| View leave balances | Employee | Real-time personal balance per absence plan at any time |
| View absence history | Employee | Full history of all absence requests and their approval status |
| Cancel leave request | Employee | Cancel a pending or approved future absence (subject to policy) |
| Approve / deny leave request | Manager | Review request in context of team calendar; approve, deny, or request modification |
| Submit absence on behalf | Manager | HR administrator or manager submits an absence entry on behalf of an employee where required |
| View team absence calendar | Manager | Full team view of approved and pending leave — visibility before approving new requests |
| Leave balance enquiry | Employee / Manager | View any team member's current balance and leave history (within data access profile) |
| Notification and alerts | All | Automated workflow notifications — request submitted, approved, denied, balance approaching limit |

##### 3.5 APPSolve Absence Management Delivery

APPSolve applies a structured delivery approach to Absence Management within every Oracle HCM implementation:

| Delivery activity | Phase | Description |
|---|---|---|
| Absence requirements workshop | Scope and Design | Capture all leave types, accrual rules, entitlements, carry-over, expiry, and payroll treatment. Document legislative requirements in standardised format. |
| Work schedule design | Scope and Design | Define standard work schedules (patterns, hours, shift patterns where applicable) — foundation for absence accruals and time calculations |
| Absence plan configuration | Build | Configure each absence plan per agreed design. Accrual rules, entitlements, eligibility profiles, qualification periods. |
| Approval workflow configuration | Build | Configure approval chains per absence type. Build notification templates. |
| OTBI absence reports | Build | Configure standard OTBI absence reports — balance reports, absence trend, leave liability, team calendar. Develop custom reports per requirements. |
| Payroll integration for absence | Build | Configure HCM Extracts or OIC interface to pass approved absence transactions to payroll platform |
| UAT — absence scenarios | Deploy | Test all absence types: standard request, carry-over, balance depletion, approval rejection, payroll calculation |
| User training | Deploy | Train employees (self-service) and managers (approvals, team calendar) during deployment |
| First-cycle support | Post go-live | Hyper-care support during first leave cycle — assist with any accrual, balance, or payroll issues arising in live operation |

---

#### Section 4: Oracle Time and Labor

##### 4.1 Overview

Oracle Time and Labor (T&L) is a comprehensive, cloud-based time management solution included within Oracle Fusion HCM. It captures, manages, and validates time worked by employees across an organisation — supporting both exempt and non-exempt workers, standard and shift-based working patterns, and complex overtime and labor compliance rules.

Oracle Time and Labor provides a flexible, rules-driven engine that enables organisations to accurately track hours worked, enforce time and attendance policies, comply with labor legislation (BCEA working time provisions), and integrate time data seamlessly with payroll, absence management, and project costing.

APPSolve implemented Oracle Time and Labor capabilities as part of a proof-of-concept programme for a South African retail client. This engagement confirmed APPSolve's functional and technical readiness to configure and deliver Oracle Time and Labor in production Oracle HCM environments.

##### 4.2 Oracle Time and Labor Capabilities

| Capability | Description |
|---|---|
| **Time entry methods** | Employees enter time via: (1) web-based timecard in the Oracle HCM self-service portal; (2) Oracle HCM Mobile App time entry; (3) physical biometric device or access control system via OIC integration; (4) manager entry on behalf of employees |
| **Configurable timecard layout** | Timecard layouts configured per working pattern — daily entry, weekly summary, project-based, cost centre-based. Fields and prompts driven by business rules. |
| **Work schedule integration** | Oracle Work Schedules define expected working patterns per employee. Time and Labor validates actual time against the expected schedule — flagging deviations for manager review. |
| **Absence integration** | Approved absences in Oracle Absence Management flow into Time and Labor automatically — absence periods appear in the timecard; no duplicate entry required. |
| **Overtime rules engine** | Configurable overtime rules — daily overtime threshold, weekly overtime threshold, shift premium rates, BCEA-compliant overtime calculation. Rules engine applies the correct overtime rate automatically. |
| **Time approval workflows** | Configurable timecard approval workflows — employee submits, line manager approves. Multi-level approvals supported. Automated reminders for missing or late timecards. |
| **Manager timecard management** | Managers view, edit (within policy), approve, and submit timecards for their team. Missing timecard alerts for direct reports. Bulk approval for teams with standard schedules. |
| **Labor policy compliance** | Enforces BCEA provisions on maximum working hours, minimum rest periods, and overtime entitlements. Policy violations flagged on the timecard before submission. |
| **Payroll integration** | Approved time data — standard hours, overtime, premiums, shift differentials — flows to Oracle Payroll Cloud or third-party payroll via HCM Extracts or OIC. Ensures accurate pay calculation based on time actually worked. |
| **Project costing integration** | Where Oracle Project Costing or Project Portfolio Management is in scope, Time and Labor passes labor hours to project cost accounts — enabling accurate project labor cost tracking. |
| **Shift differential and premium pay** | Configure shift differentials and premium pay rates (night shift, public holiday, weekend) within the Time and Labor rules engine. Applied automatically to timecards meeting the trigger conditions. |
| **Retroactive time corrections** | Corrections to submitted timecards processed retroactively — payroll recalculation triggers automatically for the affected periods. |
| **OTBI time reporting** | Pre-built OTBI subject areas for time: hours worked by employee/department/cost centre, overtime analysis, timecard completion rates, labor cost by period — cross-reference W3S1-006 for analytics. |

##### 4.3 Time and Labor Rules Engine

Oracle Time and Labor's rules-driven engine is one of its core differentiators. Complex time policies — shift premiums, overtime thresholds, public holiday rates, consecutive day rules — are configured as time rules applied automatically on each timecard.

| Rules Engine Capability | Description |
|---|---|
| **Time categories** | Define time categories (regular, overtime, shift premium, public holiday, night shift) — the basis for payroll costing and reporting |
| **Time rules** | Rules evaluate time entries against defined conditions (time of day, day of week, consecutive hours, weekly totals) and apply the correct time category automatically |
| **Shift differentials** | Shift premium rates (e.g., 25% shift allowance, 150% overtime rate, 200% public holiday rate) attached to time categories and applied by rules |
| **BCEA overtime calculation** | Oracle T&L is configured to enforce BCEA-compliant overtime: daily threshold (daily hours beyond 9 ordinary hours), weekly threshold (beyond 45 ordinary hours per week), maximum overtime limits (10 hours per week) |
| **Union/collective agreement rules** | Where collective agreements or bargaining council agreements apply, time rules encode the specific overtime, shift, and premium provisions of the applicable agreement |
| **Period-end processing** | Time is periodically processed to produce payroll-ready time data — rules evaluated for the full period, exceptions resolved before payroll runs |

##### 4.4 Time and Labor in APPSolve Implementations

**Proof-of-concept reference:**
APPSolve implemented Oracle Time and Labor capabilities as part of a proof-of-concept programme for a South African retail client. This engagement validated APPSolve's technical and functional capability to configure Oracle Time and Labor, including timecard design, rules engine configuration, and integration architecture. The client did not proceed from proof-of-concept to full production deployment.

**Active pipeline — Time and Labor delivery readiness:**
APPSolve's Oracle HCM practice includes consultants with Oracle Time and Labor configuration and delivery capability. Time and Labor is a confirmed in-scope module for Oracle HCM implementations where time tracking, overtime management, or biometric integration requirements are present.

**APPSolve T&L delivery principles:**

| Principle | Description |
|---|---|
| **No data migration** | Oracle Time and Labor does not require historical time data migration. All time entry starts fresh from go-live date. |
| **Common business rules** | T&L configuration is based on a documented, agreed set of business rules applied consistently across the Oracle HCM instance. Multiple rule sets are supported but increase configuration and testing effort. |
| **Payroll integration in scope** | The only mandatory external integration for T&L is to the payroll system. Additional integrations to time logging/access control systems are configured where a biometric or external time device is in scope. |
| **Biometric as OIC integration** | Biometric and access control system integrations are implemented as OIC interfaces — a confirmed APPSolve capability (Hollywood Bets biometric integration as precedent). |

---

#### Section 5: Workforce Scheduling

##### 5.1 Overview

Oracle Fusion Workforce Scheduling is a cloud-based workforce scheduling solution within the Oracle Fusion HCM suite. It enables organisations to manage labor resources by aligning workforce schedules with operational demands — ensuring the right employees are scheduled at the right times while maintaining compliance with labor laws, collective agreements, and organisational policies.

Oracle Workforce Scheduling is designed for industries with complex staffing requirements — retail (multi-shift, high-volume, seasonal demand), manufacturing (production scheduling, shift rotations), and healthcare (clinical and support staff rostering). It provides managers with demand-driven scheduling tools, employee self-service shift preferences, and integration with Oracle Time and Labor and Absence Management for end-to-end workforce management.

APPSolve positions Oracle Workforce Scheduling as a platform capability — APPSolve has the product knowledge and technical capability to configure and implement Oracle Workforce Scheduling where it is in scope and required by the client.

##### 5.2 Oracle Workforce Scheduling Capabilities

| Capability | Description |
|---|---|
| **Demand-driven scheduling** | Build workforce schedules aligned to operational demand patterns — staffing to peak periods, minimum coverage requirements, and labour cost targets |
| **Schedule templates** | Define shift patterns and schedule templates per department, location, or job type. Apply templates to generate baseline schedules. |
| **Employee schedule management** | Assign employees to shifts; manage shift rotations, swap requests, and schedule adjustments |
| **Self-service shift preferences** | Employees indicate shift preferences and availability windows via self-service. Scheduling engine respects preferences where operationally feasible. |
| **Shift swap and cover requests** | Employees request shift swaps or volunteer for open shifts through self-service. Manager approval workflow configurable per policy. |
| **Labor law compliance in scheduling** | Configure maximum consecutive working days, minimum rest periods between shifts, weekly hour caps, and overtime triggers within the scheduling engine. Schedules validated against these rules before publication. |
| **Collective agreement rules** | Encode collective agreement scheduling provisions — e.g., shift rotation limits, guaranteed rest periods, public holiday scheduling rules |
| **Integration with Time and Labor** | Published employee schedules drive expected time in Oracle Time and Labor. Deviations between scheduled and actual time are flagged for manager review. |
| **Integration with Absence Management** | Approved absences flow to the scheduling engine — vacant slots identified and flagged for cover. |
| **Integration with Payroll** | Schedule data (shifts, premiums, differentials) flows to payroll via Oracle Time and Labor for accurate pay calculation |
| **Labor cost optimisation** | Schedule analytics — compare scheduled labor cost against budget; identify overtime exposure; optimise staffing mix to meet coverage at minimum cost |
| **Manager schedule dashboard** | Managers view team schedules, open shifts, absence conflicts, and labor cost exposure in a single workforce dashboard |

##### 5.3 Oracle Workforce Scheduling — APPSolve Positioning

APPSolve can configure and implement Oracle Workforce Scheduling where it is identified as a client requirement during the HCM programme scoping phase.

Workforce Scheduling is particularly relevant for clients in:
- **Retail** — multi-location, variable-hours workforce; peak trading period scheduling; part-time and shift workers
- **Mining** — shift rotation management; safety-driven minimum rest period enforcement; underground vs surface scheduling
- **Manufacturing and distribution** — production shift scheduling; line and warehouse staffing
- **Healthcare** — clinical and support staff rostering; on-call management

APPSolve advises clients on Oracle Workforce Scheduling capabilities and fit during Oracle HCM programme planning. Where Workforce Scheduling is confirmed as in-scope, it is implemented as an additional workstream within the Oracle HCM programme.

### Oracle AI-Based Skills Intelligence

**Capability Statement | APPSolve | Oracle Business Unit**
*Document ID: W4-AI-002-ORA-AISkills | Version: 1.0 | Wave 4 | Approved 2026-06-14*

---

#### Section 1: Statement of Capability

APPSolve configures and implements Oracle AI-Based Skills Intelligence within Oracle Fusion HCM — Oracle's embedded artificial intelligence framework for dynamic skills profile management, AI-powered talent matching, and data-driven career development.

Oracle AI Skills is a standard capability within the Oracle HCM Cloud platform, enabling organisations to build and maintain dynamic, continuously updated skills taxonomies for every employee. APPSolve delivers AI Skills as an integrated component of Oracle Fusion HCM Talent Management implementations.

> **Confirmed implementation:** Oracle AI-Based Skills was confirmed as a delivered component of the Hollywood Bets Oracle Fusion HCM Phase 4 (Talent Management) implementation (BU Lead decision 2026-06-14).

| Capability Area | Coverage | APPSolve Positioning |
|---|---|---|
| **Dynamic Skills Profiles** | AI-generated and maintained employee skills profiles — inferred from job history, performance, learning, and role data | **Confirmed delivery capability** — AI skills profile configuration within Oracle HCM |
| **Skills Gap Analysis** | Automated identification of skills gaps against role requirements and career targets | **Confirmed delivery capability** — organisation-wide skills gap visibility |
| **AI-Powered Job Recommendations** | Oracle AI suggests internal opportunities, gigs, and career pathways based on skills profiles | **Confirmed delivery capability** — talent marketplace recommendations within HCM |
| **Skills Taxonomy Management** | Configuration of skills libraries, proficiency levels, and role-to-skill mappings | **Confirmed delivery capability** — APPSolve configures Oracle's skills taxonomy to client requirements |
| **Manager Talent Intelligence** | Aggregated team skills view for managers — identify team-level gaps, succession risks, and development priorities | **Confirmed delivery capability** — manager analytics within Oracle Talent framework |
| **Learning Integration** | AI Skills aligned with Oracle Learning Cloud (W3S1-004) for personalised learning pathway recommendations | **Confirmed delivery capability** — native integration within Oracle HCM suite |

---

#### Section 2: Product Architecture

##### 2.1 Oracle AI Skills Integration within Fusion HCM

Oracle AI Skills operates as a native intelligence layer within Oracle Fusion HCM. It requires no separate middleware or external AI platform.

```
Oracle Fusion HCM Data Sources
  ├── Global HR — job histories, roles, assignments (W3S1-001)
  ├── Performance Management — goals, ratings, competencies (W3S1-002)
  ├── Learning Cloud — completed courses, certificates (W3S1-004)
  ├── Recruiting — job profiles, requisition requirements (W3S1-003)
  └── Talent Review — potential/performance calibration (W3S1-002)
         │
         ▼
Oracle AI Skills Engine (embedded)
  ├── Skills inference — derive skills from activity data
  ├── Skills taxonomy — Oracle global skills library + client configuration
  ├── Gap analysis — role vs. actual skills comparison
  └── Recommendation engine — career paths, opportunities, learning
         │
         ▼
Oracle HCM Employee Experience
  ├── Employee: My Skills profile, career recommendations, learning suggestions
  ├── Manager: Team skills dashboard, talent risk identification
  └── HR: Organisation-wide skills analytics, workforce planning inputs
```

##### 2.2 Relationship to Oracle Talent Management Suite (W3S1-002)

Oracle AI Skills is a sub-module within the Oracle Talent Management Suite. W3S1-002 covers the broader Talent Management Suite (Performance, Goals, Talent Review, Career Development). W4-AI-002 specifically addresses the AI intelligence layer within that suite — extractable as a standalone capability where AI-specific tender requirements arise.

#### Section 5: Approved and Prohibited Wording

##### Approved Wording

> "APPSolve configures and implements Oracle AI-Based Skills Intelligence within Oracle Fusion HCM, enabling organisations to build dynamic employee skills profiles, identify skills gaps, and provide AI-powered career development recommendations."

> "APPSolve has delivered Oracle AI Skills as an integrated component of Oracle Fusion HCM Talent Management implementations, providing organisations with organisation-wide skills visibility and AI-driven talent development capabilities."

> "Oracle's embedded AI skills intelligence, configured by APPSolve, enables organisations to move from static, manually maintained skills records to dynamically inferred, AI-maintained skills profiles that improve talent decisions, succession planning, and learning investment."

##### Prohibited Wording

- Do NOT reference SAA as a client, example, or implementation (Rule 21.1)
- Do NOT reference CCBA as a client or example (HIST-014)
- Do NOT reference DFA as a client or example (Rule 21.4)
- Do NOT describe Oracle AI Skills as a standalone AI product separate from Oracle HCM — it is embedded within the Oracle HCM Cloud platform
- Do NOT conflate Oracle AI Skills with Oracle Digital Assistant (ODA) — AI Skills manages skills intelligence; ODA is a conversational chatbot
- Do NOT conflate Oracle AI Skills with Oracle Grow — Grow is a talent marketplace/gig platform; AI Skills is the intelligence layer that powers recommendations
- Do NOT describe APPSolve as an AI developer or AI platform vendor — APPSolve configures Oracle's embedded AI capabilities within Oracle HCM implementations

### Oracle Journeys — Employee Self-Service & Guided Workflows

**Capability Statement | APPSolve | Oracle Business Unit**
*Document ID: W4-HCM-002-ORA-Journeys | Version: 1.0 | Wave 4 | Approved 2026-06-14*

---

#### Section 1: Statement of Capability

APPSolve designs, configures, and implements Oracle Journeys — Oracle's guided employee self-service framework embedded within Oracle Fusion HCM. Oracle Journeys enables HR teams to build structured, personalised task checklists and guided workflows for employees navigating significant employment events and HR processes.

APPSolve delivers Oracle Journeys as an integrated component of Oracle Fusion HCM implementations, enabling organisations to standardise HR processes, reduce manual intervention, and create consistent, compliant employee experiences across the full employment lifecycle.

> **Confirmed implementation:** Oracle Journeys was confirmed as a delivered component within the Hollywood Bets Oracle Fusion HCM implementation (BU Lead decision 2026-06-14).

| Capability Area | Coverage | APPSolve Positioning |
|---|---|---|
| **Onboarding Journeys** | New employee onboarding task checklists — pre-hire, day-one, and first-90-days workflows | **Confirmed delivery capability** — standardised onboarding automation within Oracle HCM |
| **Life Event Journeys** | Employee life events — marriage, parental leave, relocation, role changes, retirement | **Confirmed delivery capability** — life event orchestration within Oracle HCM framework |
| **Offboarding Journeys** | Structured employee exit workflows — IT access revocation, equipment return, exit interviews | **Confirmed delivery capability** — compliant exit process automation |
| **HR Process Automation** | Policy acknowledgements, mandatory compliance tasks, document submission workflows | **Confirmed delivery capability** — HR policy and compliance workflow automation |
| **Personalised Employee Experience** | Role-based journey personalisation; manager and employee dual-task assignment | **Confirmed delivery capability** — audience segmentation and task personalisation |
| **Self-Service Portal Integration** | Employee self-service via Oracle Fusion HCM Me module | **Confirmed delivery capability** — integrated within Oracle HCM standard UX |

---

#### Section 2: Product Architecture

##### 2.1 Oracle Journeys Framework

Oracle Journeys is a standard Oracle Fusion HCM module available within the Oracle HCM Cloud subscription. It operates as a configured workflow engine within Oracle HCM, with no separate licensing requirement.

```
Oracle Journeys
  ├── Journey Templates (configured by APPSolve)
  │   ├── Onboarding (pre-hire → day 1 → 90 days)
  │   ├── Life Events (parental, relocation, status changes)
  │   ├── Offboarding (exit process)
  │   └── Custom HR Processes (compliance, acknowledgements)
  ├── Task Types
  │   ├── Oracle HCM native tasks (profile updates, document upload)
  │   ├── External tasks (manual completion acknowledgements)
  │   ├── Links to external systems (IT provisioning, facilities)
  │   └── DocuSign / e-signature tasks (where configured)
  ├── Assignment Rules
  │   ├── Employee (self-service)
  │   ├── Manager (manager-assigned tasks)
  │   └── HR / Specialist (HR team tasks)
  └── Analytics
      ├── Journey completion tracking
      ├── Task overdue alerting
      └── Compliance dashboards
```

##### 2.2 Integration with Oracle HCM Core

Journeys is natively embedded in Oracle HCM and does not require separate integration configuration. Triggers include:
- New hire events from Oracle Global HR (W3S1-001)
- Life event triggers from Oracle HCM benefits and HR modules
- Absence events from Oracle Workforce Management (W3S1-007)
- Recruiting hire events from Oracle Recruiting Cloud (W3S1-003)

> "APPSolve configures and implements Oracle Journeys within Oracle Fusion HCM, enabling organisations to deliver structured, guided workflows for employee onboarding, life events, offboarding, and HR compliance processes."

> "APPSolve has delivered Oracle Journeys as an integrated component of Oracle Fusion HCM implementations, providing employees with personalised, guided self-service workflows across the full employment lifecycle."

> "Oracle Journeys, implemented by APPSolve, enables HR teams to automate task orchestration for significant employment events — reducing manual HR workload while ensuring consistent, compliant employee experiences."

##### Prohibited Wording

- Do NOT reference SAA as a client, example, or implementation in any Journeys-related content (Rule 21.1)
- Do NOT reference CCBA as a client or example (HIST-014)
- Do NOT reference DFA as a client or example (Rule 21.4)
- Do NOT describe Journeys as a standalone product requiring separate Oracle licensing — it is included within the Oracle HCM Cloud subscription
- Do NOT conflate Oracle Journeys with Oracle Digital Assistant (ODA) — Journeys is a workflow tool; ODA is conversational AI
- Do NOT conflate Oracle Journeys with Oracle OAX/Experience Design Studio — different toolsets

#### Section 8: Product Boundary Controls

| Product | Relationship | Boundary Rule |
|---|---|---|
| **Oracle Journeys** | THIS STATEMENT | Guided workflow framework within Oracle HCM — task checklists, lifecycle event automation |
| **Oracle Digital Assistant (ODA)** | Different product | ODA is conversational AI for HR queries. Journeys is guided task workflow. Do NOT conflate. |
| **Oracle Application Extension (OAX)** | Different product | OAX is a UI configuration tool for Fusion pages. Journeys uses standard HCM UI. Do NOT conflate. |
| **Oracle HCM Core (W3S1-001)** | Prerequisite | Journeys is embedded within Oracle HCM. HCM Core (W3S1-001) is the mandatory prerequisite. |
| **Oracle Workforce Management (W3S1-007)** | Related | Absence events can trigger Journeys. Journeys ≠ absence management. |
| **Oracle Recruiting Cloud (W3S1-003)** | Related | Hire events can trigger onboarding Journeys. Journeys ≠ recruiting. |

## 13. Oracle Fusion ERP Capability

### Oracle Fusion Cloud Capability Statement

#### Section 1 — Oracle Fusion Platform Overview

Oracle Fusion is a suite of enterprise business applications designed to streamline and modernise enterprise processes. It integrates financial management, human capital management, supply chain, procurement, customer relationship management, and governance functions into a unified, cloud-native platform.

**Key platform characteristics:**

| Characteristic | Description |
|---|---|
| Modular Architecture | Organisations implement individual applications or the full suite, scaling as requirements evolve |
| Cloud-Native (SaaS) | Platform delivered over the internet, eliminating on-premises hardware requirements |
| Integrated Suite | Works seamlessly across all Fusion modules and with existing Oracle investments (EBS, PeopleSoft, JD Edwards) |
| Advanced Analytics | Embedded business intelligence and real-time analytics across all modules |
| User Experience | Role-based dashboards, personalised views, and mobile access for all devices |
| Global Capabilities | Multi-currency, multi-language, and multi-GAAP support for multinational operations |
| Security and Compliance | Built-in security controls, data encryption, and regulatory compliance tooling |

*Source: TMPL-001 lines 112–141; PayInc HCM lines 80–89 — identical text across both proposals confirms stable platform description*

**Oracle Fusion core component overview:**

| Module | Scope |
|---|---|
| Oracle Fusion Financials | General ledger, accounts payable, accounts receivable, fixed assets, cash management |
| Oracle Fusion Human Capital Management (HCM) | Payroll interface, talent management, workforce management, HR analytics |
| Oracle Fusion Supply Chain Management (SCM) | Procurement, inventory management, order management, product lifecycle management |
| Oracle Fusion Customer Relationship Management (CRM) | Sales automation, marketing, service, social media engagement |
| Oracle Fusion Governance, Risk and Compliance (GRC) | Risk management, policy enforcement, regulatory compliance |

*Source: TMPL-001 lines 124–141; PayInc HCM lines 91–107*

---

#### Section 3 — Oracle Fusion HCM

APPSolve is a specialist Oracle Fusion HCM implementer with multi-module, multi-sector, and multi-country delivery experience.

##### 3.1 Global Human Resources (Core HR)

Oracle Fusion Global HR centralises employee data and provides lifecycle management tools covering hiring, onboarding, job changes, transfers, and terminations. The module supports:

- Single employee master record spanning personal, position, compensation, and history data
- Real-time visual organisation charts with position management and reporting lines
- Configurable workflow approvals aligned to supervisor hierarchy
- Multi-country, multi-currency, multi-legislation employee management

**Benefits:**
- A single source of truth for all workforce data
- Elimination of duplicate administrative effort and data inconsistencies
- Foundation for all dependent HCM modules

*Source: SAA HCM RFP Section 2 (Global HR module); PayInc HCM lines 127–130, 160–164*

##### 3.2 AI-Based Dynamic Skills

Oracle Fusion AI Skills enables organisations to build and maintain a dynamic skills inventory across the workforce. The module uses AI to recommend skill development paths and align workforce capability to business objectives.

**Key features:**
- AI-driven skills profiling and gap identification
- Integration with Talent Management, Learning Cloud, and Recruiting for end-to-end workforce planning
- Dynamic skills libraries aligned to current and future role requirements

*Source: SAA HCM RFP (AI Skills module); PayInc HCM lines 130–134*

##### 3.3 Absence Management

Oracle Fusion Absence Management provides a comprehensive solution for managing all types of employee leave and absence, including:

- Configurable absence plans aligned to company policy and legislative requirements
- Employee self-service leave requests with automated approval workflows
- Integration with time management, payroll, and workforce planning for seamless absence processing
- Absence liability reporting and analytics

*Source: SAA HCM RFP (Absence Management module); PayInc HCM lines 135–139*

##### 3.4 Benefits Administration

Oracle Fusion Benefits supports the full benefits lifecycle from plan configuration through enrolment to administration. The module enables:

- Flexible plan design across medical, retirement, insurance, and voluntary benefits
- Self-service enrolment for employees with guided eligibility rules
- Integration with payroll for automated deduction processing
- Regulatory compliance and year-end reporting

*Source: SAA HCM RFP (Benefits module); PayInc HCM lines 140–144*

##### 3.5 Oracle Journeys

Oracle Journeys provides guided, personalised digital workflows for employee lifecycle events — onboarding, offboarding, role changes, and wellbeing programmes. The module:

- Assembles task lists, content, and actions across HR, IT, Facilities, and Finance
- Delivers guided experiences via desktop and mobile
- Supports custom journeys aligned to company-specific events

*Source: SAA HCM RFP (Journeys module); PayInc HCM lines 145–149*

##### 3.6 Payroll Interface

Oracle Fusion Payroll Interface provides the certified integration layer between Oracle HCM and third-party payroll systems. APPSolve has extensive experience delivering this integration across multiple clients.

**Outbound payload (HCM → Payroll):**
Locations, Positions, Jobs, Grades, Employee Master, Assignment, Salary, Leave Balances, Expenses, Overtime, Salary Increase, Bonus, Addresses, Phone Number, Tax Information, Terminations

**Return payload (Payroll → HCM):**
Payslip, IRP5, IT3A, Cost2Company Balances (for Compensation module display)

**Third-party payroll systems integrated:**
- SAP Payroll
- Deel Local Payroll
- Other third-party systems via OIC

> "APPSolve has implemented an Integration between Oracle HCM and SAP Payroll many times."

*Source: Hollywood Bets V5.0 (payroll interface field list confirmed in project scope); SAA HCM RFP line 890 (SAP Payroll statement); PayInc HCM lines 150–154*

##### 3.7 Workforce Directory Management

Oracle Fusion Workforce Directory provides employees and managers with an enterprise-grade, searchable directory of people, skills, roles, and organisational structure. Features include:

- Real-time people search with role and skills filters
- Organisational hierarchy visualisation
- Integration with Global HR for live data accuracy

*Source: SAA HCM RFP (Workforce Directory module); PayInc HCM lines 155–159*

##### 3.8 Workforce Modelling and Predictions

Oracle Fusion Workforce Modelling enables HR leaders to model and evaluate workforce restructuring scenarios, headcount changes, and organisational redesign before committing to changes. The module:

- Supports drag-and-drop organisational modelling in a sandbox environment
- Provides cost and headcount impact analysis per scenario
- Integrates with Global HR for live data and with Finance for budgetary alignment

*Source: SAA HCM RFP (Workforce Modelling module); PayInc HCM lines 160–164*

##### 3.9 Work Life Solutions

Oracle Fusion Work Life Solutions provides tools that support employee wellbeing, work-life balance, and engagement, including:

- Wellbeing tracking and goal setting
- Volunteering and charitable contribution management
- Integration with HR and absence systems for holistic employee experience

*Source: SAA HCM RFP (Work Life module); PayInc HCM lines 165–168*

##### 3.10 Oracle Transactional Business Intelligence (OTBI)

Oracle OTBI is the embedded real-time reporting and analytics tool within Oracle Fusion. Key capabilities:

- On-demand analytics with real-time data from live HR modules
- Pre-built HR reports and dashboards (headcount, turnover, compensation benchmarking)
- Ad-hoc report builder for business users without requiring IT intervention
- Data security inherits Oracle HCM role-based access controls

*Source: SAA HCM RFP (OTBI module); PayInc HCM lines 172–177*

##### 3.11 Transparent Data Encryption (TDE)

Oracle Transparent Data Encryption encrypts sensitive HR and payroll data at rest, protecting against unauthorised access at the storage layer. TDE:

- Is transparent to applications and users — no application changes required
- Encrypts data without affecting system performance
- Supports compliance with GDPR, POPIA, and other data protection regulations

*Source: SAA HCM RFP (TDE module); PayInc HCM lines 177–179*

##### 3.12 Workforce Compensation

Oracle Fusion Workforce Compensation supports merit, bonus, and equity compensation cycle management:

- Configurable compensation plans and budgets by manager, grade, or business unit
- Manager self-service compensation worksheets with guidelines and alerts
- Integration with payroll for compensation change propagation
- Total compensation statement generation

*Source: SAA HCM RFP (Workforce Compensation module)*

##### 3.13 Oracle Recruiting Cloud

Oracle Fusion Recruiting Cloud is a next-generation applicant tracking system (ATS) that supports the full talent acquisition lifecycle:

**Key features:**
- AI-powered candidate sourcing, screening, and ranking
- Branded career sites with external job posting integration
- Interview management with structured evaluation guides
- Onboarding integration — seamless candidate-to-employee transition
- Integration with Oracle Global HR, Payroll, and Workforce Management

APPSolve delivered the full Oracle Recruiting Cloud implementation for Hollywood Bets as part of its HCM transformation programme.

*Source: Hollywood Bets V5.0 (Recruiting scope confirmed); SAA HCM RFP (Recruiting module); PayInc HCM lines 184–229*

##### 3.14 Talent Management

Oracle Fusion Talent Management provides an integrated, AI-driven talent development platform covering:

- **Goal Management:** Aligns individual goals with business objectives; supports OKR-style and traditional goal frameworks
- **Performance Management:** Structured review cycles with manager and peer feedback
- **Talent Review and Succession Management:** 9-box talent assessment and succession pipeline planning
- **Career Development:** Personalised career paths, mentoring, and development plans
- AI-driven recommendations for career moves and skill development opportunities

APPSolve implemented the full Talent Management suite for Hollywood Bets including Goal Management, Performance Management, Talent Review, and Succession.

*Source: Hollywood Bets V5.0 (confirmed scope); SAA HCM RFP (Talent Management module); PayInc HCM lines 242–282*

##### 3.15 Oracle Learning Cloud

Oracle Fusion Learning Cloud is a next-generation Learning Management System (LMS) supporting formal, social, and blended learning:

- AI-personalised learning recommendations aligned to role and skills gaps
- Instructor-led, virtual, and self-paced learning support
- Integration with Oracle Talent Management and Career Development for learning-led development paths
- SETA / WSP-ATR compliance support via third-party integration (e.g., Moodle via OIC for SETA reporting)

*Source: SAA HCM RFP (Learning Cloud module); Hollywood Bets V5.0 Annexure 1 (WSP/ATR Moodle integration); PayInc HCM lines 297–341*

##### 3.16 HCM Analytics

Oracle Fusion HCM Analytics (formerly Oracle HCM Analytics Warehouse / OTBI Enterprise) delivers pre-built, cloud-based analytics extending the core HCM reporting capability:

- Pre-built dashboards for workforce composition, talent acquisition, diversity and inclusion, and employee retention
- Cross-domain analytics linking HCM data with Finance, CRM, and SCM data for holistic insights
- KPI libraries tailored for HR use cases
- Role-based security inheriting from Oracle HCM access controls

*Source: SAA HCM RFP (HCM Analytics module); PayInc HCM lines 344–377*

##### 3.17 Time and Labor / Workforce Scheduling

Oracle Fusion Time and Labor enables employees and managers to capture, approve, and process time entries against work schedules, projects, and absence policies. The module integrates with Payroll, Projects, and Absence Management for straight-through processing.

Oracle Fusion Workforce Scheduling provides advanced scheduling tools for shift-based workforces including automated schedule generation, compliance checking, and employee self-service schedule visibility.

*Source: SAA HCM RFP (Time and Labor and Workforce Scheduling modules)*

##### 3.18 HR Help Desk / Oracle Digital Assistant

Oracle HR Help Desk provides a unified case management and knowledge platform for employee HR queries. APPSolve has implemented HR Help Desk with:

- Chatbot and SMS channels for employee query submission
- Four-level routing and escalation structure (Tier 0 self-service → Tier 1 help desk → Tier 2 HR specialist → Tier 3 management escalation)
- Integration with Global HR for context-aware responses

*Source: Hollywood Bets V5.0 Annexure 2 (HR Help Desk scope and routing structure)*

#### Section 4 — Oracle Fusion ERP / Financials

Oracle Fusion Enterprise Resource Planning (ERP) is designed to manage and automate a wide range of financial and operational business processes. It is a comprehensive, cloud-based solution that integrates financial management, procurement, project management, and supply chain into a single platform.

**Oracle Fusion ERP benefits:**

| Benefit | Description |
|---|---|
| Unified Platform | Combines financial, procurement, project management, and supply chain in a single integrated system |
| Cloud-Based | Eliminates on-premises infrastructure; access from anywhere enhancing business continuity |
| Real-Time Insights | Real-time data and analytics for faster, more informed decision-making |
| Scalability | Adapts to business growth, from small enterprises to large multinational corporations |
| Automation | Automates routine tasks and processes, reducing manual effort and risk of error |
| Compliance | Supports regulatory and audit requirements, reducing non-compliance risk |

*Source: BankServAfrica ERP Proposal (August 2024) lines 391–399*

##### 4.1 Financial Management Modules

APPSolve has delivered Oracle Fusion Financials implementations across multiple clients in Southern Africa and internationally.

| Module | Description | Delivery Evidence |
|---|---|---|
| General Ledger | Centralised accounting hub supporting complex financial structures, multi-entity accounting, and real-time financial reporting | Investec (SA, UK, USA — July 2024); Nala Renewables (8-country footprint — April 2025); Cape Union Mart (Feb 2022); DFA (June 2019) |
| Accounts Payable | Automates invoice processing, vendor payments, and compliance with global tax regulations | Investec; Cape Union Mart; DFA |
| Accounts Receivable | Manages customer billing, collections, and cash application processes | Investec; Cape Union Mart; DFA |
| Fixed Assets Management | Tracks and manages the lifecycle of fixed assets, including depreciation and asset transfers | Investec; DFA |
| Cash Management | Provides visibility into cash positions, cash forecasting, and bank reconciliation | Investec; Cape Union Mart |
| iExpenses (Expense Reports) | Employee self-service expense capture, approval workflow, and integration with Accounts Payable | Investec (confirmed) |

*Source: BankServAfrica ERP Proposal lines 402–420 (module descriptions); Mpact ERP Proposal lines 500–583 (client reference cards with go-live dates and modules)*

Oracle Financials Cloud provides predefined analyses, dashboards, and reports supporting financial and business intelligence requirements. The Financial Reporting Center serves as the primary interface for all seven Oracle report types:

#### Section 5 — Oracle Fusion Procurement

Oracle Fusion Procurement is a comprehensive suite of cloud-based applications designed to streamline and enhance the procurement process. It integrates procurement activities — from supplier sourcing through contract management, purchase order execution, and invoice processing — enabling organisations to manage procurement efficiently with full policy compliance and spend visibility.

**Oracle Fusion Procurement benefits:**
- Cost Reduction: Centralising and streamlining procurement processes reduces costs and eliminates inefficiencies
- Improved Supplier Relationships: Enhanced collaboration tools foster better relationships with suppliers
- Increased Visibility: Real-time insights and analytics provide visibility into all procurement activities
- Compliance and Risk Management: Built-in contract and policy compliance reduces non-compliance and procurement risk

##### 5.1 Core Procurement Capabilities

| Capability | Description |
|---|---|
| Procurement Contracts | Manages the entire lifecycle of procurement contracts — creation, negotiation, approval, and management. Ensures compliance with organisational policies and legal requirements |
| Self-Service Procurement | Allows employees to request goods and services through a user-friendly, catalog-based interface. Reduces maverick spending by guiding employees towards approved suppliers and negotiated pricing |
| Sourcing | Facilitates strategic sourcing — supplier identification, bid collection, and bid evaluation. Supports RFQs (Request for Quotation) and reverse auctions. Enables collaboration with suppliers and internal stakeholders |
| Supplier Qualification Management | Assesses and manages supplier risk and performance. Automates the qualification process, ensuring only qualified suppliers participate in procurement activities |
| Supplier Portal | Platform for suppliers to manage profiles, view purchase orders, submit invoices, and track payments — reducing invoice processing friction for both parties |
| Spend Analysis | Analyses procurement spending to identify cost-saving opportunities. Provides insights into supplier performance, spend categories, and trends |
| Purchase Order Management | Manages creation, approval, and tracking of purchase orders. Ensures that all purchases align with contracts and organisational policies |

*Source: BankServAfrica ERP Proposal (August 2024) lines 561–604*

##### 5.2 Self-Service Procurement

Oracle Fusion Self-Service Procurement provides a consumer-like purchasing experience that empowers employees to manage their own purchasing needs while maintaining full policy compliance:

- **Consumer-like interface:** Employees search, compare, and order goods from curated catalogs of approved suppliers and products
- **Guided buying:** System routes users towards preferred suppliers and negotiated pricing, reducing off-contract spend
- **Automated approval workflows:** Requisitions automatically route for approval based on configured business rules — spending limits, departmental approvals, project-based controls
- **Real-time budget checks:** Integrates with Oracle Financials to validate budget availability before purchase commitment, preventing overspend
- **Self-service receiving:** Users confirm receipt directly in the system, automatically updating inventory and procurement records
- **Spend reporting:** Tools for managers to analyse spend patterns, supplier performance, and policy compliance

*Source: BankServAfrica ERP Proposal lines 717–805*

##### 5.3 Procurement Client Evidence

| Client | Modules | Countries | Go-Live | Reference |
|---|---|---|---|---|
| Investec | Oracle Fusion Procurement, iExpenses | SA, UK, USA (3 countries) | July 2024 | Available |
| Cape Union Mart | Oracle Fusion Procurement | South Africa | February 2022 | Available |
| DFA (Dark Fibre Africa) | Oracle SCM (iSupplier Portal, Sourcing, Contracts) | South Africa | June 2019 | **Not available** |

*Source: Mpact ERP Proposal reference cards (August 2025) lines 500–583*

#### Section 6 — Oracle Fusion Supply Chain Management (SCM)

> **SCM CAPABILITY REFERENCE ONLY — RESTRICTED USE.** APPSolve currently has no referenceable Oracle Fusion SCM client available for external tender reference. This section may be used for capability descriptions and methodology responses where delivery references are not scored criteria. Dark Fibre Africa (DFA) remains internal-use-only and may not be cited without specific BU Lead approval. BU Lead ruling applied 2026-06-11 (FR-004 — Option A).

Oracle Fusion Supply Chain Execution (SCE) is a suite of cloud-based applications managing and optimising supply chain processes — covering inventory management, order fulfilment, logistics, procurement, supply chain planning, global trade, and quality management.

**Oracle Fusion SCM benefits:**
- Improved Efficiency: Automating and optimising supply chain processes reduces costs, minimises waste, and improves throughput
- Enhanced Customer Satisfaction: On-time, accurate delivery of goods and services
- Better Decision-Making: Real-time visibility and analytics for responsive supply chain management
- Reduced Risk: Manages supplier disruptions, regulatory compliance issues, and quality problems
- Scalable Growth: Scales as supply chain operations grow without system constraints

##### 6.1 SCM Core Capabilities

| Capability | Description |
|---|---|
| Inventory Management | Real-time visibility into inventory across multiple locations — warehouses, distribution centres, retail stores. Supports multi-channel fulfilment, lot and serial tracking, inventory valuation, and accurate inventory planning |
| Order Management | Manages the entire order-to-cash process — order capture through fulfilment and invoicing. Supports drop shipping, backorders, and split shipments. Integrates with financial modules for seamless processing |
| Logistics Management | Optimises transportation and logistics; supports transportation planning, freight management, carrier integration, and real-time shipment tracking |
| Warehouse Management | Manages receiving, storage, picking, packing, and shipping. Supports advanced processes including cross-docking, wave picking, and task interleaving |
| Supply Chain Planning | Demand forecasting, supply planning, and inventory optimisation. Supports S&OP processes and scenario / what-if planning |
| Global Trade Management | Import/export compliance, customs documentation, and trade finance. Reduces risk of international trade penalties and delays |
| Quality Management | Quality standards enforcement throughout the supply chain — inspections, non-conformance management, and corrective action management |
| Maintenance | Asset and equipment maintenance management — preventive, corrective, and predictive maintenance strategies |

*Source: BankServAfrica ERP Proposal (August 2024) lines 658–715*

##### 6.2 Order Management

Oracle Fusion Order Management provides a centralised order hub for multi-channel order management — e-commerce, call centres, and partner networks. Key capabilities:

- **Order Promising:** Advanced order promising with global inventory visibility to provide accurate delivery dates
- **Configurable Workflows:** Configurable order management workflows supporting split shipments, backorders, and drop shipments
- **Pricing and Discount Management:** Tiered pricing, volume discounts, and contract-based pricing across all channels
- **Analytics and Reporting:** Real-time dashboards for order status, fulfilment performance, and customer satisfaction
- **Integration with Oracle Financials:** Invoicing, payment processing, and revenue recognition seamlessly linked to order data

*Source: BankServAfrica ERP Proposal lines 605–657*

#### Section 7 — Oracle Fusion Projects / PPM

Oracle Fusion Projects provides integrated project costing, billing, portfolio management, and project financials — supporting project-based organisations that need to track costs, recognise revenue, and manage capital expenditure across complex project portfolios.

##### 7.1 Project Financials

| Capability | Description |
|---|---|
| Budgeting and Forecasting | Create detailed project budgets and forecasts for financial planning and management |
| Cost Management | Track and control project costs — labour, materials, and overhead — ensuring projects stay within budget |
| Capital Projects | Manage capital project expenditures and asset capitalisation processes |
| Financial Reporting | Comprehensive financial reports including profit and loss, cash flow analysis, and project profitability |
| Integration with General Ledger | Seamless integration with Oracle Fusion GL for consistent and accurate financial reporting across the organisation |

*Source: BankServAfrica ERP Proposal (August 2024) lines 479–495*

##### 7.2 Project Contract Billing

| Capability | Description |
|---|---|
| Contract Management | Create and manage complex contracts — terms, conditions, and billing arrangements |
| Billing Rules | Flexible billing methods — fixed-price, time and materials, milestone-based billing |
| Revenue Recognition | Automated revenue recognition in compliance with accounting standards |
| Invoice Processing | Automated invoice creation and processing based on contract terms and project progress |
| Customer Collaboration | Customer portals for contract approval, invoice tracking, and dispute resolution |

*Source: BankServAfrica ERP Proposal lines 460–477*

##### 7.3 Project Management

| Capability | Description |
|---|---|
| Project Planning | Define project scope, objectives, timelines, and resources using structured planning tools |
| Task Management | Break down projects into tasks, assign responsibilities, track progress to completion |
| Resource Management | Allocate and manage resources — personnel, equipment, materials — to optimise project efficiency |
| Collaboration | Integrated collaboration tools — document sharing and discussion forums across project teams |
| Project Monitoring and Control | Real-time dashboards and analytics for proactive management and risk mitigation |
| Issue and Risk Management | Identify and manage project risks and issues to avoid delays |

*Source: BankServAfrica ERP Proposal lines 496–516*

---

#### Section 8 — Oracle Analytics

APPSolve's Oracle Analytics capability spans both embedded and standalone analytics platforms:

**Oracle Transactional Business Intelligence (OTBI):**
Real-time, self-service reporting embedded within every Oracle Fusion module. Business users access on-demand dashboards, ad-hoc reports, and KPI views without IT dependency. Role-based security ensures data access aligns with Oracle Fusion user roles.

**Oracle Fusion HCM Analytics:**
Pre-built, cloud-based analytics extending HCM reporting capability with dedicated KPI libraries for workforce composition, talent acquisition, diversity and inclusion, and employee retention. Supports cross-domain analytics linking HCM with Finance and other Fusion modules.

**Oracle Business Intelligence (OBI):**
Where clients require enterprise-grade BI beyond embedded analytics, APPSolve deploys Oracle Business Intelligence solutions including dashboards, scorecards, and data warehouse integration.

*Source: SAA HCM RFP (OTBI and HCM Analytics modules); PayInc HCM lines 344–377; ORACLE_FACT_BASELINE.md Section 9*

---

#### Section 9 — Oracle Integration Cloud (OIC)

Oracle Integration Cloud (OIC) is Oracle's strategic Integration Platform as a Service (iPaaS) solution, specifically designed for integrating Oracle Cloud applications with other cloud and on-premises systems.

##### OIC as APPSolve Standard

Oracle Integration Cloud is a mandatory component in every APPSolve Oracle Fusion implementation. OIC is deployed in all Oracle Fusion projects for all inbound and outbound interfaces between Oracle SaaS and third-party systems.

> "All our Fusion implementation we have also implemented Oracle Integration Cloud. We have used OIC for all inbound and out bound interfaces between Oracle SaaS and 3rd party systems."

*Source: RedPath Mining RFI line 195*

##### OIC Core Capabilities

| Capability | Description |
|---|---|
| Pre-built Adapters | Oracle HCM, ERP, SCM, CX; SAP, Salesforce, Workday, and 400+ third-party adaptors |
| Visual Designer | Low-code / no-code visual designer for integrations, transformations, and orchestrations |
| Process Automation | Automates business processes spanning multiple applications |
| REST API / SOAP Support | Full API integration capability for custom and legacy system connectivity |
| HDL / HSDL / FBDI | Oracle-native bulk data load integrations for HCM and Financials |

*Source: PayInc HCM lines 379–384 (OIC description and adaptor capability); RedPath Mining RFI line 195*

##### Integration Patterns Delivered

**HCM integrations:**
- Oracle HCM ↔ SAP Payroll (confirmed: SAA June 2025, "many times")
- Oracle HCM ↔ Deel Local Payroll (PayInc)
- Oracle HCM ↔ Moodle (WSP/ATR SETA reporting, Hollywood Bets)
- Oracle HCM ↔ Third-party payroll via full payroll interface field set

**Financials and Procurement integrations:**
- Oracle Fusion Finance ↔ third-party banking (HDL/FBDI patterns)
- Oracle Fusion Finance ↔ external reporting systems

**Multi-client OIC deployments confirmed:**
DFA, Cape Union Mart, Hollywood Bets, Mr Price, Investec, Nala — all confirmed OIC via RedPath Mining RFI

*Source: SAA HCM RFP line 890 (SAP Payroll); Hollywood Bets V5.0 (Moodle integration via OIC); RedPath Mining RFI line 195 and client list lines 243–249; PayInc HCM*

---

#### Section 10 — Security and Compliance

APPSolve implements Oracle Cloud's full security stack as part of every Fusion deployment, ensuring clients meet data protection, access control, and regulatory compliance requirements.

**Oracle Cloud Security controls deployed:**

| Control | Description |
|---|---|
| Oracle Cloud Guard | Continuous cloud security posture monitoring and automated remediation |
| Web Application Firewall (WAF) | Layer 7 protection against web-based attacks |
| Identity and Access Management (IAM) | Role-based access control with Oracle Fusion module-level security |
| Transparent Data Encryption (TDE) | At-rest encryption for all sensitive HR and financial data |
| Multi-Factor Authentication (MFA) | Mandatory MFA for all Oracle Cloud user access |

**Regulatory and compliance alignment:**
- GDPR compliance tooling embedded in Oracle Fusion
- POPIA data subject management via Oracle HCM privacy controls
- SOC 1 and SOC 2 certifications (Oracle Cloud Infrastructure)

*Source: SAA HCM RFP lines 1096–1109 (OCI security controls — Cloud Guard, WAF, IAM, TDE, MFA); PayInc HCM lines 177–179 (TDE)*

> **Exclusion note:** OCI platform infrastructure capabilities (compute, storage, networking) are excluded from this statement per W2S1-001 scope. Security controls listed are those deployed at the application and data layer within Oracle Fusion implementations.

---

#### Section 11 — Mobile Experience

Oracle Fusion provides a responsive, mobile-first user experience across all modules, enabling employees, managers, and administrators to complete HR, finance, and operational tasks from any device.

**Mobile capabilities:**

| Capability | Access |
|---|---|
| Employee Self-Service (ESS) | Leave requests, payslip access, profile updates, absence capture |
| Manager Self-Service (MSS) | Approval workflows, team dashboards, performance reviews |
| Oracle Digital Assistant | AI-powered chatbot accessible via mobile for HR query resolution |
| Oracle Workforce Scheduling | Mobile shift management and schedule visibility |
| Mobile Recruiting | Candidate review, interview scheduling, and offer approvals on mobile |

*Source: TMPL-001 line 119 (mobile access emphasis); SAA HCM RFP (Workforce Scheduling module); PayInc HCM line 87 (mobile access statement); Hollywood Bets V5.0 (HR Help Desk chatbot)*
